class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr6-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to subsection&nbsp;(2), a court before which proceedings are brought to enforce a liability which is limited by Article&nbsp;22 in the First, Second or Third Schedule shall, where the liability is, or may be, partly enforceable in other proceedings in Singapore or elsewhere, have jurisdiction&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to award an amount less than the court would have awarded if the limitation applied solely to the proceedings before the court; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to make any part of its award conditional on the result of any other proceedings.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr6-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, from time to time specify the respective amounts which, for the purposes of Article&nbsp;22 in the First, Second and Third Schedules, are to be taken as equivalent to the sums expressed in francs or Special Drawing Rights, as the case may be, which are mentioned in that Article.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr6-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;References in this section to Article&nbsp;22 in the First and Third Schedules shall, subject to any necessary modifications, include references to that Article as applied by Article&nbsp;25A in the First and Third Schedules respectively.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr7-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Notice of partial loss</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>7.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In Article&nbsp;26(2) in the First, Second and Third Schedules, the references to damage shall be construed as including loss of part of the baggage or cargo in question and the references to the receipt of baggage or cargo shall, in relation to loss of part of it, be construed as receipt of the remainder of it.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr8-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Time for bringing proceedings</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>8.</strong><a name="pr8-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;No action against a carrier’s employee or agent which arises out of damage to which the Warsaw Convention, the Warsaw (Hague) Convention or the Warsaw (Hague) (Montreal) Convention relates shall, if he was acting within the scope of his employment, be brought after more than 2 years, reckoned from the date of arrival at the destination or from the date on which the aircraft ought to have arrived, or from the date on which the carriage stopped.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></span><a name="pr8-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;29 in the First, Second and Third Schedules shall not be read as applying to any proceedings for contribution between persons liable for any damage to which the Warsaw Convention, the Warsaw (Hague) Convention or the Warsaw (Hague) (Montreal) Convention relates.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr8-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to sections&nbsp;4 and 29 of the Limitation Act (Cap. 163), no action shall be brought by a person, liable for any damage to which the Warsaw Convention, the Warsaw (Hague) Convention or the Warsaw (Hague) (Montreal) Convention relates, to recover contribution from any other person in respect of the damage after the expiration of 2 years from the time when a court gives judgment or makes an award against the person seeking to recover the contribution.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr8-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subsections&nbsp;(1), (2) and (3) and Article&nbsp;29 in the First, Second and Third Schedules shall have effect as if references in those provisions to an action included references to an arbitration.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt" id="pr8-ps5-">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;[<em>Deleted by Act 41/2007 wef 16/11/2007</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr9-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Contributory negligence</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>9.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;It is declared that, for the purposes of Article&nbsp;21 in the First, Second and Third Schedules, the provisions of the Contributory Negligence and Personal Injuries Act (Cap. 54) are provisions of the law of Singapore under which a court may exonerate the carrier wholly or partly from his liability.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr10-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to exclude aircraft in use for military purposes</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>10.</strong><a name="pr10-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, direct that this section shall apply, or shall cease to apply, to Singapore or any other State specified in the order.</span><a name="pr10-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Warsaw (Hague) Convention and the Warsaw (Hague) (Montreal) Convention shall not apply to the carriage of persons, cargo and baggage for the military authorities of a State to which this section applies in aircraft registered in that State if the whole capacity of the aircraft has been reserved by or on behalf of those authorities.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Actions against High Contracting Parties</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11.</strong><a name="pr11-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every High Contracting Party to the Warsaw Convention, the Warsaw (Hague) Convention or the Warsaw (Hague) (Montreal) Convention who has not availed himself of the provisions of the Additional Protocol at the end of the First, Second or Third Schedule shall, for the purposes of any action brought in a court in Singapore in accordance with Article&nbsp;28 in the First, Second or Third Schedule to enforce a claim in respect of carriage undertaken by him, be deemed to have submitted to the jurisdiction of that court, and accordingly the Rules of Court (Cap. 322, R 5) may provide for the manner in which any action is to be commenced and carried on.</span><a name="pr11-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this section shall authorise the issue of execution against the property of any High Contracting Party.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Application to carriage by air not governed by Warsaw (Hague) Convention and Warsaw (Hague) (Montreal) Convention</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may make regulations applying the provisions of the First and Third Schedules and any provision of this Act to such carriage by air, not being international carriage as defined in the First and Third Schedules, as may be specified in the regulations, subject to such exceptions, adaptations and modifications, if any, as may be specified.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr13-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Application to Government</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>13.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act shall bind the Government.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="schedule"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sHdr" id="Sc1-">FIRST SCHEDULE</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="SbodyRefs" id="Sc1-rf-">Section&nbsp;2</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="scHdr" id="Sc1-he-">The Warsaw Convention with the amendments made to it by the Hague Protocol</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">(Words in square brackets in the text are words substituted for or added to the original Warsaw Convention by Chapter I of the Hague Protocol).</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc1-S2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdr" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">CONVENTION FOR THE UNIFICATION OF CERTAIN RULES <br>RELATING TO INTERNATIONAL CARRIAGE BY AIR</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S11-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter 1</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Scope — Definitions</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S11-S21_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 1</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention applies to all international carriage of persons, baggage or cargo performed by aircraft for reward. It applies equally to gratuitous carriage by aircraft performed by an air transport undertaking.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this Convention, the expression <em>international carriage</em> means any carriage in which, according to the agreement between the parties, the place of departure and the place of destination, whether or not there be a break in the carriage or a transhipment, are situated either within the territories of two High Contracting Parties or within the territory of a single High Contracting Party if there is an agreed stopping place within the territory of another State, even if that State is not a High Contracting Party. Carriage between two points within the territory of a single High Contracting Party without an agreed stopping place within the territory of another State is not international carriage for the purposes of this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Carriage to be performed by several successive air carriers is deemed, for the purposes of this Convention, to be one undivided carriage if it has been regarded by the parties as a single operation, whether it had been agreed upon under the form of a single contract or of a series of contracts, and it does not lose its international character merely because one contract or a series of contracts is to be performed entirely within the territory of the same State.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S11-S22_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 2</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention applies to carriage performed by the State or by legally constituted public bodies provided it falls within the conditions laid down in Article&nbsp;1.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention shall not apply to carriage of mail and postal packages.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1II-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter II</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Documents of Carriage<p></p>Section 1 — Passenger Ticket</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1II-S23_2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 3</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In respect of the carriage of passengers a ticket shall be delivered containing:</td></tr></tbody></table><table class="p1_1" style="font-size:11pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">an indication of the places of departure and destination;</td></tr><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">if the places of departure and destination are within the territory of a single High Contracting Party, one or more agreed stopping places being within the territory of another State, an indication of at least one such stopping place;</td></tr><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">a notice to the effect that, if the passenger’s journey involves an ultimate destination or stop in a country other than the country of departure, the Warsaw Convention may be applicable and that the Convention governs and in most cases limits the liability of carriers for death or personal injury and in respect of loss of or damage to baggage.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The passenger ticket shall constitute <em>prima facie</em> evidence of the conclusion and conditions of the contract of carriage. The absence, irregularity or loss of the passenger ticket does not affect the existence or the validity of the contract of carriage which shall, none the less, be subject to the rules of this Convention. Nevertheless, if, with the consent of the carrier, the passenger embarks without a passenger ticket having been delivered, or if the ticket does not include the notice required by paragraph (1) (<em>c</em>) of this Article, the carrier shall not be entitled to avail himself of the provisions of Article&nbsp;22.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Section 2 — Baggage Check</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc2-S24_2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 4</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In respect of the carriage of registered baggage, a baggage check shall be delivered, which, unless combined with or incorporated in a passenger ticket which complies with the provisions of Article&nbsp;3, paragraph (1), shall contain:</td></tr></tbody></table><table class="p1_1" style="font-size:11pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">an indication of the places of departure and destination;</td></tr><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">if the places of departure and destination are within the territory of a single High Contracting Party, one or more agreed stopping places being within the territory of another State, an indication of at least one such stopping place;</td></tr><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">a notice to the effect that, if the carriage involves an ultimate destination or stop in a country other than the country of departure, the Warsaw Convention may be applicable and that the Convention governs and in most cases limits the liability of carriers in respect of loss of or damage to baggage.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The baggage check shall constitute <em>prima facie</em> evidence of the registration of the baggage and of the conditions of the contract of carriage. The absence, irregularity or loss of the baggage check does not affect the existence or the validity of the contract of carriage which shall, none the less, be subject to the rules of this Convention. Nevertheless, if the carrier takes charge of the baggage without a baggage check having been delivered or if the baggage check (unless combined with or incorporated in the passenger ticket which complies with the provisions of Article&nbsp;3, paragraph (1) (<em>c</em>)) does not include the notice required by paragraph (1) (<em>c</em>) of this Article, he shall not be entitled to avail himself of the provisions of Article&nbsp;22, paragraph (2).]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Section 3 — Air Waybill</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S25_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 5</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every carrier of cargo has the right to require the consignor to make out and hand over to him a document called an “air waybill”; every consignor has the right to require the carrier to accept this document.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The absence, irregularity or loss of this document does not affect the existence or the validity of the contract of carriage which shall, subject to the provisions of Article&nbsp;9, be none the less governed by the rules of this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S26_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 6</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The air waybill shall be made out by the consignor in 3 original parts and be handed over with the cargo.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The first part shall be marked “for the carrier”, and shall be signed by the consignor. The second part shall be marked “for the consignee”; it shall be signed by the consignor and by the carrier and shall accompany the cargo. The third part shall be signed by the carrier and handed by him to the consignor after the cargo has been accepted.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The carrier shall sign prior to the loading of the cargo on board the aircraft.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The signature of the carrier may be stamped; that of the consignor may be printed or stamped.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;If, at the request of the consignor, the carrier makes out the air waybill, he shall be deemed, subject to proof to the contrary, to have done so on behalf of the consignor.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S27-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 7</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The carrier of cargo has the right to require the consignor to make out separate waybills when there is more than one package.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S28-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 8</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[The air waybill shall contain:</td></tr></tbody></table><table class="p1_1" style="font-size:11pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">an indication of the places of departure and destination;</td></tr><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">if the places of departure and destination are within the territory of a single High Contracting Party, one or more agreed stopping places being within the territory of another State, an indication of at least one such stopping place;</td></tr><tr><td class="sGrpP1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="sGrpP1">a notice to the consignor to the effect that, if the carriage involves an ultimate destination or stop in a country other than the country of departure, the Warsaw Convention may be applicable and that the Convention governs and in most cases limits the liability of carriers in respect of loss of or damage to cargo.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S29-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 9</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[If, with the consent of the carrier, cargo is loaded on board the aircraft without an air waybill having been made out, or if the air waybill does not include the notice required by Article&nbsp;8, paragraph (<em>c</em>), the carrier shall not be entitled to avail himself of the provisions of Article&nbsp;22, paragraph (2).]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S210_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 10</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The consignor is responsible for the correctness of the particulars and statements relating to the cargo which he inserts in the air waybill.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The consignor shall indemnify the carrier against all damage suffered by him, or by any other person to whom the carrier is liable, by reason of the irregularity, incorrectness or incompleteness of the particulars and statements furnished by the consignor.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S211_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 11</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The air waybill is <em>prima facie</em> evidence of the conclusion of the contract, of the receipt of the cargo and of the conditions of carriage.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The statements in the air waybill relating to the weight, dimensions and packing of the cargo, as well as those relating to the number of packages, are <em>prima facie</em> evidence of the facts stated; those relating to the quantity, volume and condition of the cargo do not constitute evidence against the carrier except so far as they both have been and are stated in the air waybill to have been, checked by him in the presence of the consignor, or relate to the apparent condition of the cargo.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S212_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 12</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to his liability to carry out all his obligations under the contract of carriage, the consignor has the right to dispose of the cargo by withdrawing it at the aerodrome of departure or destination, or by stopping it in the course of the journey on any landing, or by calling for it to be delivered at the place of destination or in the course of the journey to a person other than the consignee named in the air waybill, or by requiring it to be returned to the aerodrome of departure. He must not exercise this right of disposition in such a way as to prejudice the carrier or other consignors and he must repay any expenses occasioned by the exercise of this right.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;If it is impossible to carry out the orders of the consignor the carrier must so inform him forthwith.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;If the carrier obeys the orders of the consignor for the disposition of the cargo without requiring the production of the part of the air waybill delivered to the latter, he will be liable, without prejudice to his right of recovery from the consignor, for any damage which may be caused thereby to any person who is lawfully in possession of that part of the air waybill.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The right conferred on the consignor ceases at the moment when that of the consignee begins in accordance with Article&nbsp;13. Nevertheless, if the consignee declines to accept the air waybill or the cargo, or if he cannot be communicated with, the consignor resumes his right of disposition.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S213_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 13</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Except in the circumstances set out in the preceding Article, the consignee is entitled, on arrival of the cargo at the place of destination, to require the carrier to hand over to him the air waybill and to deliver the cargo to him, on payment of the charges due and on complying with the conditions of carriage set out in the air waybill.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Unless it is otherwise agreed, it is the duty of the carrier to give notice to the consignee as soon as the cargo arrives.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;If the carrier admits the loss of the cargo, or if the cargo has not arrived at the expiration of 7 days after the date on which it ought to have arrived, the consignee is entitled to put into force against the carrier the rights which flow from the contract of carriage.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S214-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 14</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The consignor and the consignee can respectively enforce all the rights given them by Articles&nbsp;12 and 13, each in his own name, whether he is acting in his own interest or in the interest of another, provided that he carries out the obligations imposed by the contract.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S215_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 15</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Articles&nbsp;12, 13 and 14 do not affect either the relations of the consignor or the consignee with each other or the mutual relations of third parties whose rights are derived either from the consignor or from the consignee.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The provisions of Articles&nbsp;12, 13 and 14 can only be varied by express provision in the air waybill.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Convention prevents the issue of a negotiable air waybill.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc3-S216_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 16</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The consignor must furnish such information and attach to the air waybill such documents as are necessary to meet the formalities of customs, octroi or police before the cargo can be delivered to the consignee. The consignor is liable to the carrier for any damage occasioned by the absence, insufficiency or irregularity of any such information or documents, unless the damage is due to the fault of the carrier or his servants or agents.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The carrier is under no obligation to enquire into the correctness or sufficiency of such information or documents.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter III</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Liability of the Carrier</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S217-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 17</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The carrier is liable for damage sustained in the event of the death or wounding of a passenger or any other bodily injury suffered by a passenger, if the accident which caused the damage so sustained took place on board the aircraft or in the course of any of the operations of embarking or disembarking.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S218_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 18</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The carrier is liable for damage sustained in the event of the destruction or loss of, or of damage to, any registered baggage or any cargo, if the occurrence which caused the damage so sustained took place during the carriage by air.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The carriage by air within the meaning of the preceding paragraph comprises the period during which the baggage or cargo is in charge of the carrier, whether in an aerodrome or on board an aircraft, or, in the case of a landing outside an aerodrome, in any place whatsoever.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The period of the carriage by air does not extend to any carriage by land, by sea or by river performed outside an aerodrome. If, however, such a carriage takes place in the performance of a contract for carriage by air, for the purpose of loading, delivery or transhipment, any damage is presumed, subject to proof to the contrary, to have been the result of an event which took place during the carriage by air.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S219-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 19</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The carrier is liable for damage occasioned by delay in the carriage by air of passengers, baggage or cargo.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S220-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 20</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The carrier is not liable if he proves that he and his servants and agents have taken all necessary measures to avoid the damage or that it was impossible for him and them to take such measures.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S221-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 21</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">If the carrier proves that the damage was caused by or contributed to by the negligence of the injured person the court may, in accordance with the provisions of its own law, exonerate the carrier wholly or partly from his liability.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S222_2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 22</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the carriage of persons the liability of the carrier for each passenger is limited to the sum of 250,000 francs. Where, in accordance with the law of the court seised of the case, damages may be awarded in the form of periodical payments, the equivalent capital value of the said payments shall not exceed 250,000 francs. Nevertheless, by special contract, the carrier and the passenger may agree to a higher limit of liability.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a name="Sc1-S1III-S222_2-s12-p1a-"></a>(<em>a</em>)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the carriage of registered baggage and of cargo, the liability of the carrier is limited to a sum of 250 francs per kilogramme, unless the passenger or consignor has made, at the time when the package was handed over to the carrier, a special declaration of interest in delivery at destination and has paid a supplementary sum if the case so requires. In that case the carrier will be liable to pay a sum not exceeding the declared sum, unless he proves that that sum is greater than the passenger’s or consignor’s actual interest in delivery at destination.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(<em>b</em>)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of loss, damage or delay of part of registered baggage or cargo, or of any object contained therein, the weight to be taken into consideration in determining the amount to which the carrier’s liability is limited shall be only the total weight of the package or packages concerned. Nevertheless, when the loss, damage or delay of a part of the registered baggage or cargo or of an object contained therein, affects the value of other packages covered by the same baggage check or the same air waybill, the total weight of such package or packages shall also be taken into consideration in determining the limit of liability.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;As regards objects of which the passenger takes charge himself the liability of the carrier is limited to 5,000 francs per passenger.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The limits prescribed in this Article shall not prevent the court from awarding, in accordance with its own law, in addition, the whole or part of the court costs and of the other expenses of the litigation incurred by the plaintiff. The foregoing provision shall not apply if the amount of the damages awarded, excluding court costs and other expenses of the litigation, does not exceed the sum which the carrier has offered in writing to the plaintiff within a period of 6 months from the date of the occurrence causing the damage, or before the commencement of the action, if that is later.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;The sums mentioned in francs in this Article shall be deemed to refer to a currency unit consisting of 65<sup>1</sup>/<sub>2</sub> milligrammes of gold of millesimal fineness 900. These sums may be converted into national currencies in round figures. Conversion of the sums into national currencies other than gold shall, in case of judicial proceedings, be made according to the gold value of such currencies at the date of the judgment.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S223_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 23</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any provision tending to relieve the carrier of liability or to fix a lower limit than that which is laid down in this Convention shall be null and void, but the nullity of any such provision does not involve the nullity of the whole contract, which shall remain subject to the provisions of this Convention.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Paragraph (1) of this Article shall not apply to provisions governing loss or damage resulting from the inherent defect, quality or vice of the cargo carried.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S224_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 24</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the cases covered by Articles&nbsp;18 and 19 any action for damages, however founded, can only be brought subject to the conditions and limits set out in this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the cases covered by Article&nbsp;17 the provisions of the preceding paragraph also apply, without prejudice to the questions as to who are the persons who have the right to bring suit and what are their respective rights.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S225-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 25</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[The limits of liability specified in Article&nbsp;22 shall not apply if it is proved that the damage resulted from an act or omission of the carrier, his servants or agents, done with intent to cause damage or recklessly and with knowledge that damage would probably result; provided that, in the case of such act or omission of a servant or agent, it is also proved that he was acting within the scope of his employment.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S225A_2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 25A</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;If an action is brought against a servant or agent of the carrier arising out of damage to which this Convention relates, such servant or agent, if he proves that he acted within the scope of his employment, shall be entitled to avail himself of the limits of liability which that carrier himself is entitled to invoke under Article&nbsp;22.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The aggregate of the amounts recoverable from the carrier, his servants and agents, in that case, shall not exceed the said limits.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The provisions of paragraphs (1) and (2) of this Article shall not apply if it is proved that the damage resulted from an act or omission of the servant or agent done with intent to cause damage or recklessly and with knowledge that damage would probably result.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S226_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 26</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Receipt by the person entitled to delivery of baggage or cargo without complaint is <em>prima facie</em> evidence that the same has been delivered in good condition and in accordance with the document of carriage.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of damage, the person entitled to delivery must complain to the carrier forthwith after the discovery of the damage, and, at the latest, within 7 days from the date of receipt in the case of baggage and 14 days from the date of receipt in the case of cargo. In the case of delay the complaint must be made at the latest within 21 days from the date on which the baggage or cargo has been placed at his disposal.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every complaint must be made in writing upon the document of carriage or by separate notice in writing despatched within the times aforesaid.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Failing complaint within the times aforesaid, no action shall lie against the carrier, save in the case of fraud on his part.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S227-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 27</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">In the case of the death of the person liable, an action for damages lies in accordance with the terms of this Convention against those legally representing his estate.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S228_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 28</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;An action for damages must be brought, at the option of the plaintiff, in the territory of one of the High Contracting Parties, either before the court having jurisdiction where the carrier is ordinarily resident, or has his principal place of business, or has an establishment by which the contract has been made or before the court having jurisdiction at the place of destination.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Questions of procedure shall be governed by the law of the court seised of the case.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S229_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 29</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The right to damages shall be extinguished if an action is not brought within two years, reckoned from the date of arrival at the destination, or from the date on which the aircraft ought to have arrived, or from the date on which the carriage stopped.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The method of calculating the period of limitation shall be determined by the law of the court seised of the case.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1III-S230_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 30</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of carriage to be performed by various successive carriers and falling within the definition set out in the third paragraph of Article&nbsp;1, each carrier who accepts passengers, baggage or cargo is subjected to the rules set out in this Convention, and is deemed to be one of the contracting parties to the contract of carriage in so far as the contract deals with that part of the carriage which is performed under his supervision.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of carriage of this nature, the passenger or his representative can take action only against the carrier who performed the carriage during which the accident or the delay occurred, save in the case where, by express agreement, the first carrier has assumed liability for the whole journey.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;As regards baggage or cargo, the passenger or consignor will have a right of action against the first carrier, and the passenger or consignee who is entitled to delivery will have a right of action against the last carrier, and further, each may take action against the carrier who performed the carriage during which the destruction, loss, damage or delay took place. These carriers will be jointly and severally liable to the passenger or to the consignor or consignee.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1IV-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter IV</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Provisions Relating to Combined Carriage</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1IV-S231_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 31</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of combined carriage performed partly by air and partly by any other mode of carriage, the provisions of this Convention apply only to the carriage by air, provided that the carriage by air falls within the terms of Article&nbsp;1.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Convention shall prevent the parties in the case of combined carriage from inserting in the document of air carriage conditions relating to other modes of carriage, provided that the provisions of this Convention are observed as regards the carriage by air.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter V</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">General and Final Provisions</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S232-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 32</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">Any clause contained in the contract and all special agreements entered into before the damage occurred by which the parties purport to infringe the rules laid down by this Convention, whether by deciding the law to be applied, or by altering the rules as to jurisdiction, shall be null and void. Nevertheless for the carriage of cargo arbitration clauses are allowed, subject to this Convention, if the arbitration is to take place within one of the jurisdictions referred to in the first paragraph of Article&nbsp;28.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S233-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 33</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">Nothing contained in this Convention shall prevent the carrier either from refusing to enter into any contract of carriage, or from making regulations which do not conflict with the provisions of this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S234-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 34</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[The provisions of Articles&nbsp;3 to 9 inclusive relating to documents of carriage shall not apply in the case of carriage performed in extraordinary circumstances outside the normal scope of an air carrier’s business.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S235-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 35</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The expression “days” when used in this Convention means current days not working days.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S236-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 36</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The Convention is drawn up in French in a single copy which shall remain deposited in the archives of the Ministry for Foreign Affairs of Poland and of which one duly certified copy shall be sent by the Polish Government to the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S237_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 37</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention shall be ratified. The instruments of ratification shall be deposited in the archives of the Ministry for Foreign Affairs of Poland, which will notify the deposit to the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;As soon as this Convention shall have been ratified by 5 of the High Contracting Parties it shall come into force as between them on the ninetieth day after the deposit of the fifth ratification. Thereafter it shall come into force between the High Contracting Parties who shall have ratified and the High Contracting Party who deposits his instrument of ratification on the ninetieth day after the deposit.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;It shall be the duty of the Government of the Republic of Poland to notify to the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties the date on which this Convention comes into force as well as the date of the deposit of each ratification.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S238_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 38</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention shall, after it has come into force, remain open for accession by any State.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The accession shall be effected by a notification addressed to the Government of the Republic of Poland, which will inform the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties thereof.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The accession shall take effect as from the ninetieth day after the notification made to the Government of the Republic of Poland.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S239_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 39</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any one of the High Contracting Parties may denounce this Convention by a notification addressed to the Government of the Republic of Poland, which will at once inform the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Denunciation shall take effect 6 months after the notification of denunciation, and shall operate only as regards the Party who shall have proceeded to denunciation.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S240_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 40</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any High Contracting Party may, at the time of signature or of deposit of ratification or of accession declare that the acceptance which he gives to this Convention does not apply to all or any of his colonies, protectorates, territories under mandate, or any other territory subject to his sovereignty or his authority, or any territory under his suzerainty.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Accordingly any High Contracting Party may subsequently accede separately in the name of all or any of his colonies, protectorates, territories under mandate or any other territory subject to his sovereignty or to his authority or any territory under his suzerainty which has been thus excluded by his original declaration.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any High Contracting Party may denounce this Convention, in accordance with its provisions, separately or for all or any of his colonies, protectorates, territories under mandate or any other territory subject to his sovereignty or to his authority, or any other territory under his suzerainty.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S240A_2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 40A</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In Article&nbsp;37, paragraph (2), and Article&nbsp;40, paragraph (1), the expression High Contracting Party shall mean <em>State</em>. In all other cases, the expression High <em>Contracting Party</em> shall mean a State whose ratification of or adherence to the Convention has become effective and whose denunciation thereof has not become effective.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of the Convention the word <em>territory</em> means not only the metropolitan territory of a State but also all other territories for the foreign relations of which that State is responsible.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1V-S241-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 41</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">Any High Contracting Party shall be entitled not earlier than two years after the coming into force of this Convention to call for the assembling of a new international Conference in order to consider any improvements which may be made in this Convention. To this end he will communicate with the Government of the French Republic which will take the necessary measures to make preparations for such Conference.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxtSO" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">This Convention done at Warsaw on the 12th October 1929, shall remain open for signature until the 31st January 1930.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc4-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Additional Protocol</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc1-S1-oc4-S2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">(With reference to Article 2)</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpSTxt1" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">The High Contracting Parties reserve to themselves the right to declare at the time of ratification or of accession that paragraph&nbsp;(1) of Article&nbsp;2 of this Convention shall not apply to international carriage by air performed directly by the State, its colonies, protectorates or mandated territories or by any other territory under its sovereignty, suzerainty or authority.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="schedule"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sHdr" id="Sc2-">SECOND SCHEDULE</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="SbodyRefs" id="Sc2-rf-">Section&nbsp;2</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="scHdr" id="Sc2-he-">The Unamended Warsaw Convention</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Convention for the Unification of Certain Rules Relating to International Carriage by Air</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1I-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter I</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Scope — Definitions</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1I-S21_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 1</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention applies to all international carriage of persons, baggage or cargo performed by aircraft for reward. It applies equally to gratuitous carriage by aircraft performed by an air transport undertaking.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this Convention, the expression “international carriage” means any carriage in which, according to the agreement between the parties, the place of departure and the place of destination, whether or not there be a break in the carriage or a transhipment, are situated either within the territories of two High Contracting Parties, or within the territory of a single High Contracting Party, if there is an agreed stopping place within a territory subject to the sovereignty, suzerainty, mandate or authority of another Power, even though that Power is not a party to this Convention. A carriage without such an agreed stopping place between territories subject to the sovereignty, suzerainty, mandate or authority of the same High Contracting Party is not deemed to be international for the purposes of this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Carriage to be performed by several successive air carriers is deemed, for the purposes of this Convention, to be one undivided carriage, if it has been regarded by the parties as a single operation, whether it had been agreed upon under the form of a single contract or of a series of contracts, and it does not lose its international character merely because one contract or a series of contracts is to be performed entirely within a territory subject to the sovereignty, suzerainty, mandate or authority of the same High Contracting Party.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1I-S22_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 2</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Convention applies to carriage performed by the State or by legally constituted public bodies provided it falls within the conditions laid down in Article&nbsp;1.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention does not apply to carriage performed under the terms of any international postal Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1II-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter II</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Documents of Carriage<p></p>Section 1 — Passenger Ticket</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1II-S23_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 3</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the carriage of passengers the carrier must deliver a passenger ticket which shall contain the following particulars:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:11pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the place and date of issue;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the place of departure and of destination;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the agreed stopping places, provided that the carrier may reserve the right to alter the stopping places in case of necessity, and that if he exercises that right, the alteration shall not have the effect of depriving the carriage of its international character;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the name and address of the carrier or carriers;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">a statement that the carriage is subject to the rules relating to liability established by this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The absence, irregularity or loss of the passenger ticket does not affect the existence or the validity of the contract of carriage, which shall none the less be subject to the rules of this Convention. Nevertheless, if the carrier accepts a passenger without a passenger ticket having been delivered he shall not be entitled to avail himself of those provisions of this Convention which exclude or limit his liability.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Section 2 — Baggage Check</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc2-S24_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 4</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the carriage of baggage, other than small personal objects of which the passenger takes charge himself, the carrier must deliver a baggage check.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The baggage check shall be made out in duplicate, one part for the passenger and the other part for the carrier.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The baggage check shall contain the following particulars:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:11pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the place and date of issue;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the place of departure and of destination;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the name and address of the carrier or carriers;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the number of the passenger ticket;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">a statement that delivery of the baggage will be made to the bearer of the baggage check;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the number and weight of the packages;</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">the amount of the value declared in accordance with Article&nbsp;22(2);</td></tr><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>h</em>)</td><td class="sProvP1">a statement that the carriage is subject to the rules relating to liability established by this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The absence, irregularity or loss of the baggage check does not affect the existence or the validity of the contract of carriage, which shall none the less be subject to the rules of this Convention. Nevertheless, if the carrier accepts baggage without a baggage check having been delivered, or if the baggage check does not contain the particulars set out at (<em>d</em>), (<em>f</em>) and (<em>h</em>) above, the carrier shall not be entitled to avail himself of those provisions of the Convention which exclude or limit his liability.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc3-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Section 3 — Air Waybill</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc3-S25_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 5</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every carrier of cargo has the right to require the consignor to make out and hand over to him a document called an “air waybill”; every consignor has the right to require the carrier to accept this document.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The absence, irregularity or loss of this document does not affect the existence or the validity of the contract of carriage which shall, subject to the provisions of Article&nbsp;9, be none the less governed by the rules of this Convention.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc3-S26_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 6</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The air waybill shall be made out by the consignor in 3 original parts and be handed over with the cargo.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The first part shall be marked “for the carrier”, and shall be signed by the consignor. The second part shall be marked “for the consignee”; it shall be signed by the consignor and by the carrier and shall accompany the cargo. The third part shall be signed by the carrier and handed by him to the consignor after the cargo has been accepted.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The carrier shall sign on acceptance of the cargo.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The signature of the carrier may be stamped; that of the consignor may be printed or stamped.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;If, at the request of the consignor, the carrier makes out the air waybill, he shall be deemed, subject to proof to the contrary, to have done so on behalf of the consignor.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc3-S27_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 7</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>The carrier of cargo has the right to require the consignor to make out separate air waybills when there is more than one package.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc2-S1-oc3-S28_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 8</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>The air waybill shall contain the following particulars:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:11pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sProvP1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td
