Such limits of liability constitute maximum limits and may not be exceeded whatever the circumstances which gave rise to the liability.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S2_-oc2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">[Article 25</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>In the carriage of passengers and baggage, the limits of liability specified in Article&nbsp;22 shall not apply if it is proved that the damage resulted from an act or omission of the carrier, his servants or agents, done with intent to cause damage or recklessly and with knowledge that damage would probably result; provided that, in the case of such act or omission of a servant or agent, it is also proved that he was acting within the scope of his employment.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S225A_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 25A</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;If an action is brought against a servant or agent of the carrier arising out of damage to which this Convention relates, such servant or agent, if he proves that he acted within the scope of his employment, shall be entitled to avail himself of the limits of liability which that carrier himself is entitled to invoke under Article&nbsp;22.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The aggregate of the amounts recoverable from the carrier, his servants and agents, in that case, shall not exceed the said limits.<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sTxtNoNum" style="text-align: justify;text-indent:0.097222in;font-size:11pt;">[(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the carriage of passengers and baggage, the provisions of paragraphs (1) and (2) of this Article shall not apply if it is proved that the damage resulted from an act or omission of the servant or agent done with intent to cause damage or recklessly and with knowledge that damage would probably result.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S226_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 26</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Receipt by the person entitled to delivery of baggage or cargo without complaint is <em>prima facie</em> evidence that the same has been delivered in good condition and in accordance with the document of carriage.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of damage, the person entitled to delivery must complain to the carrier forthwith after the discovery of the damage, and, at the latest, within 7 days from the date of receipt in the case of baggage and 14 days from the date of receipt in the case of cargo. In the case of delay the complaint must be made at the latest within 21 days from the date on which the baggage or cargo has been placed at his disposal.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every complaint must be made in writing upon the document of carriage or by separate notice in writing despatched within the times aforesaid.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Failing complaint within the times aforesaid, no action shall lie against the carrier, save in the case of fraud on his part.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S227_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 27</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>In the case of the death of the person liable, an action for damages lies in accordance with the terms of this Convention against those legally representing his estate.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S228_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 28</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;An action for damages must be brought, at the option of the plaintiff, in the territory of one of the High Contracting Parties, either before the court having jurisdiction where the carrier is ordinarily resident, or has his principal place of business, or has an establishment by which the contract has been made or before the court having jurisdiction at the place of destination.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Questions of procedure shall be governed by the law of the court seised of the case.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S229_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 29</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The right to damages shall be extinguished if an action is not brought within two years, reckoned from the date of arrival at the destination, or from the date on which the aircraft ought to have arrived, or from the date on which the carriage stopped.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The method of calculating the period of limitation shall be determined by the law of the court seised of the case.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S230_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 30</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of carriage to be performed by various successive carriers and falling within the definition set out in the third paragraph of Article&nbsp;1, each carrier who accepts passengers, baggage or cargo is subjected to the rules set out in this Convention, and is deemed to be one of the contracting parties to the contract of carriage in so far as the contract deals with that part of the carriage which is performed under his supervision.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of carriage of this nature, the passenger or his representative can take action only against the carrier who performed the carriage during which the accident or the delay occurred, save in the case where, by express agreement, the first carrier has assumed liability for the whole journey.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;As regards baggage or cargo, the passenger or consignor will have a right of action against the first carrier, and the passenger or consignee who is entitled to delivery will have a right of action against the last carrier, and further, each may take action against the carrier who performed the carriage during which the destruction, loss, damage or delay took place. These carriers will be jointly and severally liable to the passenger or to the consignor or consignee.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1III-S2_-oc3-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">[Article 30A</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>Nothing in this Convention shall prejudice the question whether a person liable for damage in accordance with its provisions has a right of recourse against any other person.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1IV-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter IV</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Provisions Relating to Combined Carriage</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1IV-S231_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 31</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of combined carriage performed partly by air and partly by any other mode of carriage, the provisions of this Convention apply only to the carriage by air, provided that the carriage by air falls within the terms of Article&nbsp;1.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Convention shall prevent the parties in the case of combined carriage from inserting in the document of air carriage conditions relating to other modes of carriage, provided that the provisions of this Convention are observed as regards the carriage by air.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><div style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Chapter V</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">General and Final Provisions</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S232_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 32</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>Any clause contained in the contract and all special agreements entered into before the damage occurred by which the parties purport to infringe the rules laid down by this Convention, whether by deciding the law to be applied, or by altering the rules as to jurisdiction, shall be null and void. Nevertheless for the carriage of cargo arbitration clauses are allowed, subject to this Convention, if the arbitration is to take place within one of the jurisdiction referred to in the first paragraph of Article&nbsp;28.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S2_-oc1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">[Article 33</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>Except as provided in paragraph&nbsp;(3) of Article&nbsp;5, nothing in this Convention shall prevent the carrier either from refusing to enter into any contract of carriage or from making regulations which do not conflict with the provisions of this Convention.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S2_-oc2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">[Article 34</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>The provisions of Articles&nbsp;3 to 8 inclusive relating to documents of carriage shall not apply in the case of carriage performed in extraordinary circumstances outside the normal scope of an air carrier’s business.]</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S235_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 35</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>The expression “days” when used in this Convention means current days not working days.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S236_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 36</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>The Convention is drawn up in French in a single copy which shall remain deposited in the archives of the Ministry for Foreign Affairs of Poland and of which one duly certified copy shall be sent by the Polish Government to the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S237_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 37</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention shall be ratified. The instruments of ratification shall be deposited in the archives of the Ministry for Foreign Affairs of Poland, which will notify the deposit to the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;As soon as this Convention shall have been ratified by 5 of the High Contracting Parties it shall come into force as between them on the ninetieth day after the deposit of the fifth ratification. Thereafter it shall come into force between the High Contracting Parties who shall have ratified and the High Contracting Party who deposits his instrument of ratification on the ninetieth day after the deposit.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;It shall be the duty of the Government of the Republic of Poland to notify to the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties the date on which this Convention comes into force as well as the date of the deposit of each ratification.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S238_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 38</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Convention shall, after it has come into force, remain open for accession by any State.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The accession shall be effected by a notification addressed to the Government of the Republic of Poland, which will inform the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties thereof.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The accession shall take effect as from the ninetieth day after the notification made to the Government of the Republic of Poland.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S239_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 39</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any one of the High Contracting Parties may denounce this Convention by a notification addressed to the Government of the Republic of Poland, which will at once inform the Government of each of the High Contracting Parties.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Denunciation shall take effect 6 months after the notification of denunciation, and shall operate only as regards the Party who shall have proceeded to denunciation.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S240_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 40</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any High Contracting Party may, at the time of signature or of deposit of ratification or of accession declare that the acceptance which he gives to this Convention does not apply to all or any of his colonies, protectorates, territories under mandate, or any other territory subject to his sovereignty or his authority, or any territory under his suzerainty.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Accordingly any High Contracting Party may subsequently accede separately in the name of all or any of his colonies, protectorates, territories under mandate or any other territory subject to his sovereignty or to his authority or any territory under his suzerainty which has been thus excluded by his original declaration.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any High Contracting Party may denounce this Convention, in accordance with its provisions, separately or for all or any of his colonies, protectorates, territories under mandate or any other territory subject to his sovereignty or to his authority, or any other territory under his suzerainty.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S240A_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 40A</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In Article&nbsp;37, paragraph (2), and Article&nbsp;40, paragraph (1), the expression <em>High Contracting Party</em> shall mean <em>State</em>. In all other cases, the expression High <em>Contracting Party</em> shall mean a State whose ratification of or adherence to the Convention has become effective and whose denunciation thereof has not become effective.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of the Convention the word territory means not only the metropolitan territory of a State but also all other territories for the foreign relations of which that State is responsible.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1V-S241_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">Article 41</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>Any High Contracting Party shall be entitled not earlier than two years after the coming into force of this Convention to call for the assembling of a new international Conference in order to consider any improvements which may be made in this Convention. To this end he will communicate with the Government of the French Republic which will take the necessary measures to make preparations for such Conference.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>This Convention done at Warsaw on the 12th October 1929, shall remain open for signature until the 31st January 1930.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1-oc5-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrCaps" style="text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:uppercase;font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;">Additional Protocol</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="Sc3-S1-oc5-S2_-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="" style="margin-top:0.2in;margin-bottom:0.2in;text-align:center"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpHdrIta" style="text-align:center;text-transform:none;"><span style="font-style:normal; font-size:11pt;"></span><span style="text-transform:none;font-style:italic; font-size:11pt;">(With reference to Article 2)</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="tailSTxt"><span class="sProvDot"></span>The High Contracting Parties reserve to themselves the right to declare at the time of ratification or of accession that paragraph&nbsp;(1) of Article&nbsp;2 of this Convention shall not apply to international carriage by air performed directly by the State, its colonies, protectorates or mandated territories or by any other territory under its sovereignty, suzerainty or authority.<div class="amendNote">[7/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="12c6c410-eb57-4c21-a4de-0967bebdc547"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="0daf669b-92df-47e2-ba50-4bc0c5c005a1"></div></div>
<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Choice of Court Agreements Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 39A)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 14 of 2016)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2017</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(30 November 2017)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to give effect to the Convention on Choice of Court Agreements done at The Hague on 30 June 2005 and for connected purposes.<sup>&nbsp;</sup><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="FN"><sup>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</sup> This revised edition incorporates all amendments up to 1 November 2017.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[1 October 2016]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P11-"><div class="partNo">PART 1</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P11-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title </span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act is the Choice of Court Agreements Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">General interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong><a name="pr2-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“chosen court” means a court, of a Contracting State, designated in an exclusive choice of court agreement;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Contracting State”&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">means a State that is a party to the Convention; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">includes, in an appropriate case&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdContractingState-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">a Regional Economic Integration Organisation that is a party to the Convention; and</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdContractingState-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">a member State, of a Regional Economic Integration Organisation that is a party to, and has made a declaration under Article&nbsp;30(1) of, the Convention;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Convention” means the Convention on Choice of Court Agreements done at The Hague on 30 June 2005;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“court of origin”, in relation to a foreign judgment for which recognition or enforcement is sought under this Act, means the court that has given the foreign judgment;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“foreign judgment” means a judgment given by a court of a Contracting State (other than Singapore), being&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a chosen court; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a court to which a chosen court has transferred, in accordance with the law or practice relating to the allocation of jurisdiction or transfer of cases among courts in that Contracting State, the case to which the judgment relates;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“judgment” means&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a final court decision (by whatever name called) on the merits, a consent order, a consent judgment or a judgment given by default; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a determination by a court of any costs or expenses relating to any such court decision, consent order, consent judgment or judgment given by default;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“judicial settlement”&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">means a contract approved by, or concluded before, a court of a Contracting State (other than Singapore), in the course of proceedings, being a contract&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdjudicialsettlement-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">between the parties to proceedings before that court;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdjudicialsettlement-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">by which those parties end those proceedings; and</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdjudicialsettlement-p1a-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">that is recorded by that court in an official document; but</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">does not include a consent order or consent judgment;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“law of Singapore” means any written law or any rule of law that applies in Singapore;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“State of origin”&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in relation to a foreign judgment for which recognition or enforcement is sought under this Act, means the Contracting State of the court of origin of the foreign judgment; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in relation to a judicial settlement for which enforcement is sought under this Act, means the Contracting State of the court that recorded the judicial settlement.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr2-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the High Court is designated in an exclusive choice of court agreement, the designation is to be construed as including the Singapore International Commercial Court unless a contrary intention appears in the agreement.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Unless the context otherwise requires, where different systems of law apply in different territorial units in a Contracting State (other than a Regional Economic Integration Organisation)&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any reference to the law or procedure of that Contracting State is to be construed as a reference, where appropriate, to the law or procedure in force in the relevant territorial unit of that Contracting State;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any reference to residence in that Contracting State is to be construed as a reference, where appropriate, to residence in the relevant territorial unit of that Contracting State;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any reference to the court or courts of that Contracting State is to be construed as a reference, where appropriate, to the court or courts in the relevant territorial unit of that Contracting State; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any reference to a connection with that Contracting State is to be construed as a reference, where appropriate, to a connection with the relevant territorial unit of that Contracting State.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Meaning of “exclusive choice of court agreement”</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong><a name="pr3-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;An exclusive choice of court agreement is an agreement between 2 or more parties that&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is concluded or documented&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr3-ps1-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">in writing; or</td></tr><tr id="pr3-ps1-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">by any other means of communication that renders the information communicated accessible so as to be usable for subsequent reference; and</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">designates, for the purpose of deciding any dispute that arises or may arise in connection with a particular legal relationship, the courts, or one or more specific courts, of one Contracting State to the exclusion of the jurisdiction of any other court.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr3-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;A choice of court agreement between 2 or more parties that satisfies the following requirements is deemed to be an exclusive choice of court agreement, unless the parties to the agreement expressly provide otherwise:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the agreement is concluded or documented&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr3-ps2-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">in writing; or</td></tr><tr id="pr3-ps2-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">by any other means of communication that renders the information communicated accessible so as to be usable for subsequent reference;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the agreement designates, for the purpose of deciding any dispute that arises or may arise in connection with a particular legal relationship, the courts, or one or more specific courts, of one Contracting State.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Meaning of “international case”</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of Part&nbsp;2, a case is an international case unless&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the parties to the case reside in the same Contracting State; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the relationship of the parties and all other elements relevant to the dispute (other than the location of the chosen court) are connected only with that Contracting State.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of Part&nbsp;3, a case is an international case if the claim is for&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the recognition, or recognition and enforcement, of a foreign judgment; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the enforcement of a judicial settlement recorded before a court of a Contracting State (other than Singapore).</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Exclusive choice of court agreement as independent agreement</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an exclusive choice of court agreement forms part of a contract&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the agreement is to be treated as independent of the other terms of the contract; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the validity of the agreement cannot be challenged solely on the ground that the contract is not valid.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Residence of person other than individual</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this Act, a person (other than an individual) is resident in a State if&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person has its statutory seat in that State;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person was incorporated or formed under the law of that State;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person has its central administration in that State; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person has its principal place of business in that State.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr7-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Act binds Government</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>7.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act binds the Government.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr8-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Application of Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>8.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to sections&nbsp;9, 10 and 22, this Act applies in every international case where there is an exclusive choice of court agreement concluded in a civil or commercial matter.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr9-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Certain matters excluded from Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>9.</strong><a name="pr9-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act does not apply to an exclusive choice of court agreement if&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any party to the agreement is an individual who acts primarily in the capacity of a consumer; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the agreement relates to a contract of employment or a collective agreement.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr9-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act does not apply to any of the following matters:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the status and legal capacity of an individual;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any matter relating to family law, including&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">the rights or obligations arising out of a marriage or a similar relationship;</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">divorce or the annulment or dissolution of a marriage;</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1b-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">maintenance;</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1b-p2iv-"><td class="p2No">(iv)</td><td class="p2Txt">matrimonial property; and </td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1b-p2v-"><td class="p2No">(v)</td><td class="p2Txt">the custody of children;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any matter relating to succession, including wills, intestate succession, the provision of maintenance for a spouse or child of a deceased individual out of the deceased individual’s estate, the administration of estates and other probate matters;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">bankruptcy, insolvency, composition or any analogous matter;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the carriage of passengers and goods;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any matter relating to any of the following:<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1f-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">marine pollution;</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1f-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">limitation of liability for a maritime claim;</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1f-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">general average;</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps2-p1f-p2iv-"><td class="p2No">(iv)</td><td class="p2Txt">emergency towage and salvage;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any matter relating to competition or anti‑trust law;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>h</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">liability for nuclear damage;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>i</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any claim for personal injury or death brought by or on behalf of an individual;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>j</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any tort or delict claim, for damage to any movable or immovable tangible property, that does not arise from a contractual relationship;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>k</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any right in rem in any immovable property or any tenancy of immovable property;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>l</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the validity, nullity or dissolution of any legal person, or the validity of a decision of the management of the legal person;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>m</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the validity of any intellectual property right (other than copyright and related rights);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>n</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the infringement of any intellectual property right (other than copyright and related rights) except any infringement proceedings that are or could have been brought for breach of a contract between the parties relating to that intellectual property right;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>o</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the validity of an entry in a public register.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act does not apply to an arbitration or any proceeding related to an arbitration.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may by regulations made under section&nbsp;22&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">exclude from the application of this Act&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr9-ps4-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">any specific matter; or</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps4-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">any specific matter in relation to any Contracting State; or</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">modify the application of this Act or any provision of this Act to&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr9-ps4-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">any specific matter; or</td></tr><tr id="pr9-ps4-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">any specific matter in relation to any Contracting State.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;Despite subsections&nbsp;(2) and (4)(<em>a</em>), the raising in any court proceedings of a matter mentioned in subsection&nbsp;(2) or (4)(<em>a</em>) as a preliminary question or defence, and not as an object of the proceedings, does not prevent this Act from applying to those proceedings.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;A proceeding under a contract of insurance or reinsurance is not excluded from the application of this Act by reason only that the contract relates to a matter to which this Act does not apply.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&nbsp;&nbsp;A proceeding is not excluded from the application of this Act by reason only that a State (including a government, a government agency or any person acting for a State) is a party to the proceeding.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps8-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(8)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act does not affect the privileges and immunities of a State or an international organisation, in respect of the State or international organisation and of its property.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr10-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Act does not apply to interim measures of protection </span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>10.</strong><a name="pr10-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act does not apply to any interim measure of protection.</span><a name="pr10-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">this Act does not prevent a party from applying to a Singapore court for an interim measure of protection in any case or proceeding involving an exclusive choice of court agreement; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">this Act does not prevent a Singapore court from granting, in any such case or proceeding, any interim measure of protection under the law of Singapore.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="c8a18bca-8913-404d-b797-d37f241e95bd"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="1b5dfd42-f80f-4360-b3e5-fbc39f1946f9"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="90ad5aeb-96b3-4fa3-8959-0f24a5999b23"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="dd9db051-ebf6-4f49-87f7-6d87b738de5a-XX"></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="dms"
