the place where the originator has its place of business and is deemed to be received at the place where the addressee has its place of business.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr13-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subsections&nbsp;(2), (3) and (4) shall apply notwithstanding that the place where the information system supporting an electronic address is located may be different from the place where the electronic communication is deemed to be received under subsection&nbsp;(5).<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 15; UN, Art. 10]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr14-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Invitation to make offer</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>14.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;A proposal to conclude a contract made through one or more electronic communications which is not addressed to one or more specific parties, but is generally accessible to parties making use of information systems, including a proposal that makes use of interactive applications for the placement of orders through such information systems, is to be considered as an invitation to make offers, unless it clearly indicates the intention of the party making the proposal to be bound in case of acceptance.<div class="sourceNote">[UN, Art. 11]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr15-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Use of automated message systems for contract formation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>15.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;A contract formed by the interaction of an automated message system and a natural person, or by the interaction of automated message systems, shall not be denied validity or enforceability solely on the ground that no natural person reviewed or intervened in each of the individual actions carried out by the automated message systems or the resulting contract.<div class="sourceNote">[UN, Art. 12]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr16-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Error in electronic communications</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>16.</strong><a name="pr16-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a natural person makes an input error in an electronic communication exchanged with the automated message system of another party and the automated message system does not provide the person with an opportunity to correct the error, that person, or the party on whose behalf that person was acting, has the right to withdraw the portion of the electronic communication in which the input error was made.</span><a name="pr16-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subsection&nbsp;(1) shall not apply unless the person, or the party on whose behalf that person was acting&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">notifies the other party of the error as soon as possible after having learned of the error and indicates that he made an error in the electronic communication; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">has not used or received any material benefit or value from the goods or services, if any, received from the other party.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr16-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this section shall affect the application of any rule of law that may govern the consequences of any error other than as provided for in subsections&nbsp;(1) and (2).<div class="sourceNote">[UN, Art. 14]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1III-"><div class="partNo">PART III</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1III-he-">SECURE ELECTRONIC RECORDS AND SIGNATURES</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr17-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Secure electronic record</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>17.</strong><a name="pr17-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;If a specified security procedure, or a commercially reasonable security procedure agreed to by the parties involved, has been properly applied to an electronic record to verify that the electronic record has not been altered since a specific point in time, such record shall be treated as a secure electronic record from such specific point in time to the time of verification.</span><a name="pr17-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this section and section&nbsp;18, whether a security procedure is commercially reasonable shall be determined having regard to the purposes of the procedure and the commercial circumstances at the time the procedure was used, including&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the nature of the transaction;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the sophistication of the parties;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the volume of similar transactions engaged in by either or all parties;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the availability of alternatives offered to but rejected by any party;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the cost of alternative procedures; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the procedures in general use for similar types of transactions.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 16]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr18-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Secure electronic signature</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>18.</strong><a name="pr18-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;If, through the application of a specified security procedure, or a commercially reasonable security procedure agreed to by the parties involved, it can be verified that an electronic signature was, at the time it was made&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">unique to the person using it;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">capable of identifying such person;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">created in a manner or using a means under the sole control of the person using it; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">linked to the electronic record to which it relates in a manner such that if the record was changed the electronic signature would be invalidated,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">such signature shall be treated as a secure electronic signature<em>.</em></td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr18-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Whether a security procedure is commercially reasonable shall be determined in accordance with section&nbsp;17(2).<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 17]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr19-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Presumptions relating to secure electronic records and signatures</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>19.</strong><a name="pr19-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In any proceedings involving a secure electronic record, it shall be presumed, unless evidence to the contrary is adduced, that the secure electronic record has not been altered since the specific point in time to which the secure status relates.</span><a name="pr19-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In any proceedings involving a secure electronic signature, it shall be presumed, unless evidence to the contrary is adduced, that&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the secure electronic signature is the signature of the person to whom it correlates; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the secure electronic signature was affixed by that person with the intention of signing or approving the electronic record.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr19-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;In the absence of a secure electronic record or a secure electronic signature, nothing in this Part shall create any presumption relating to the authenticity and integrity of the electronic record or electronic signature.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 18]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1IV-"><div class="partNo">PART IV</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1IV-he-">REGULATION OF SPECIFIED SECURITY PROCEDURES AND SPECIFIED SECURITY PROCEDURE PROVIDERS</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr20-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation of this Part</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>20.</strong><a name="pr20-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Part, “designated person” means any member of a class of specified security procedure providers specified in the Fourth&nbsp;Schedule.</span><a name="pr20-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the avoidance of doubt, a reference to this Part shall include a reference to the Second, Third and Fourth Schedules.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr21-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Specified security procedures</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>21.</strong><a name="pr21-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, amend the Second&nbsp;Schedule to add, delete or modify any specified security procedure for the purposes of this Act.</span><a name="pr21-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The provisions set out in the Third Schedule shall apply to the corresponding specified security procedures.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr21-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, amend the Third Schedule to make provisions relating to any of the specified security procedures, including&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">specifying the conditions under which any electronic signature may be treated as a secure electronic signature;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">specifying the conditions under which any electronic record may be treated as a secure electronic record;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">prescribing the effect of and duties relating to the use of specified security procedures, including the rights and duties of any persons relating to the use of such procedures and specifying rules relating to the presumptions, assumption of risk, foreseeability of reliance and liability limits applicable to the use of specified security procedures; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">prescribing offences in respect of the contravention of any provision in that Schedule, and prescribing fines not exceeding $20,000 or imprisonment which may not exceed 2 years or both, that may, on conviction, be imposed in respect of any such offence.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr21-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, amend the Fourth&nbsp;Schedule.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr22-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Regulation of specified security procedures and specified security procedure providers</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>22.</strong><a name="pr22-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may make regulations for the carrying out of this Part and, without prejudice to such general power, may make regulations for all or any of the following purposes:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the regulation, licensing or accreditation of specified security procedure providers and their authorised representatives;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">safeguarding or maintaining the effectiveness and efficiency of the common security infrastructure relating to the use of secure electronic signatures and the authentication of electronic records, including the imposition of requirements to ensure interoperability between specified security procedure providers or in relation to any security procedure;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">ensuring that the common security infrastructure relating to the use of secure electronic signatures and the authentication of electronic records complies with Singapore’s international obligations;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">prescribing the forms and fees applicable for the purposes of this Part.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr22-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to the generality of subsection&nbsp;(1), the Minister may, in making regulations for the regulation, licensing or accreditation of specified security procedure providers and their authorised representatives&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">prescribe the accounts to be kept by specified security procedure providers;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">provide for the appointment and remuneration of an auditor, and for the costs of an audit carried out under the regulations;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">provide for the establishment and regulation of any electronic system by a specified security procedure provider, whether by itself or in conjunction with other specified security procedure providers, and for the imposition and variation of requirements or conditions relating thereto as the Controller may think fit;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">make provisions to ensure the quality of repositories and the services they provide, including provisions for the standards, licensing or accreditation of repositories;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">provide for the use of any accreditation mark in relation to the activities of specified security procedure providers and for controls over the use thereof;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">prescribe the duties and liabilities of specified security procedure providers registered, licensed or accredited under this Act in respect of their customers; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">provide for the conduct of any inquiry into the conduct of specified security procedure providers and their authorised representatives and the recovery of the costs and expenses involved in such an inquiry.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr22-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to the generality of subsection&nbsp;(1), the Minister may make regulations to provide for the cross-border recognition of specified security procedure providers or specified security procedures or any processes or records related thereto, including any requirements&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">relating to interoperability arrangements with the specified security procedure providers;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">whether the specified security procedure providers satisfy certain requirements applicable to specified security procedure providers registered, accredited or licensed under this Act;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">whether the specified security procedures, processes or records satisfy certain requirements applicable to specified security procedures, processes or records (as the case may be) under this Act;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">that the processes or records have been guaranteed by a specified security procedure provider registered, accredited or licensed under this Act;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">that&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr22-ps3-p1e-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">the specified security procedure providers have been registered, accredited or licensed;</td></tr><tr id="pr22-ps3-p1e-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the processes have been specified; or</td></tr><tr id="pr22-ps3-p1e-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the records have been registered,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1SO" style="font-size:13pt">under a particular registration, accreditation or licensing scheme (as the case may be) established outside Singapore; or</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">that the specified security procedure providers, specified security procedures, processes or records have been recognised under a particular bilateral or multilateral agreement with Singapore.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr22-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Regulations made under this section may provide that a contravention of a specified provision shall be an offence and may provide penalties for a fine not exceeding $50,000 or imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months or both.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, ss. 42, 43 and 46]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr23-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Controller may give directions for compliance</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>23.</strong><a name="pr23-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller may, by notice in writing, direct any designated person, or any officer, employee or authorised representative of a designated person&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to take such measures or stop carrying on such activities as are specified in the notice if they are necessary to ensure compliance with this Part; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to co-operate with any other designated persons or public agencies as the Controller thinks necessary in the case of a public emergency.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr23-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who fails to comply with any direction specified in a notice issued under subsection&nbsp;(1) shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $50,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months or to both.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr23-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;If any doubt arises as to the existence of a public emergency for the purposes of subsection&nbsp;(1)(<em>b</em>), a certificate signed by the Minister delivered to the designated person shall be conclusive evidence of the matters stated therein.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 51]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr24-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to investigate</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>24.</strong><a name="pr24-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller or an authorised officer may investigate the activities of any designated person, or any officer, employee or authorised representative of a designated person, in relation to their compliance with this Part.</span><a name="pr24-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of subsection&nbsp;(1), the Controller may in writing issue an order to any designated person, or any officer, employee or authorised representative of a designated person, to further an investigation under this section or to secure compliance with this Part, including an order to produce records, accounts, data and documents kept by the designated person, and to allow the Controller or an authorised officer to examine and copy any of them.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, ss. 52 and 55(a)]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1V-"><div class="partNo">PART V</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1V-he-">USE OF ELECTRONIC RECORDS <br>AND SIGNATURES BY PUBLIC AGENCIES</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr25-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Acceptance of electronic filing and issue of documents</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>25.</strong><a name="pr25-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any public agency that, pursuant to any written law&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">accepts the filing of documents, or obtains information in any form;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt"><em> </em>requires that documents be created or retained;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">requires documents, records or information to be provided or retained in their original form;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">issues any permit, licence or approval; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">requires payment of any fee, charge or other amount by any method and manner of payment,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">may, notwithstanding anything to the contrary in such written law, carry out that function by means of electronic records or in electronic form.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr25-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In any case where a public agency decides to perform any of the functions in subsection&nbsp;(1) by means of electronic records or in electronic form, the public agency may specify&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the manner and format in which such electronic records shall be filed, created, retained<em>,</em> issued or provided;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where such electronic records have to be signed, the type of electronic signature required (including, if applicable, a requirement that the sender use a particular type of secure electronic signature);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the manner and format in which such signature shall be affixed to the electronic record, and the identity of or criteria that shall be met by any specified security procedure provider used by the person filing the document;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">such control processes and procedures as may be appropriate to ensure adequate integrity, security and confidentiality of electronic records or payments; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any other required attributes for electronic records or payments that are currently specified for corresponding paper documents.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr25-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the avoidance of doubt, notwithstanding anything to the contrary in any written law but subject to any specification made under subsection&nbsp;(2), where any person is required by any written law to&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">file any document with or provide information in any form to a public agency;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">create or retain any document for a public agency;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">use a prescribed form for an application or notification to, or other transaction with, a public agency;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">provide to or retain for a public agency any document, record or information in its original form; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">hold a licence, permit or other approval from a public agency,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">such a requirement is satisfied by an electronic record specified by the public agency for that purpose and&nbsp;—</td></tr></tbody></table><table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(i)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case of a requirement referred to in paragraph&nbsp;(<em>a</em>), (<em>c</em>) or (<em>d</em>), transmitted or retained (as the case may be) in the manner specified by the public agency;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(ii)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case of a requirement referred to in paragraph&nbsp;(<em>b</em>), created or retained (as the case may be) in the manner specified by the public agency; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(iii)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case of a requirement referred to in paragraph&nbsp;(<em>e</em>), issued by the public agency.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr25-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to sections&nbsp;9 and 10, nothing in this Act shall by itself compel any public agency to accept or issue any document or information in the form of electronic records or to accept any payment in electronic form.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 47]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1VI-"><div class="partNo">PART VI</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1VI-he-">LIABILITY OF NETWORK SERVICE PROVIDERS</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr26-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Liability of network service providers</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>26.</strong><a name="pr26-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to subsection&nbsp;(2), a network service provider shall not be subject to any civil or criminal liability under any rule of law in respect of third-party material in the form of electronic records to which he merely provides access if such liability is founded on&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the making, publication, dissemination or distribution of such materials or any statement made in such material; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the infringement of any rights subsisting in or in relation to such material.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr26-ps1A-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(1A)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to subsection&nbsp;(2), a network service provider shall not be subject to any liability under the Personal Data Protection Act&nbsp;2012 in respect of third-party material in the form of electronic records to which he merely provides access.<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2012 wef 02/01/2013]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr26-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this section shall affect&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any obligation founded on contract;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the obligation of a network service provider as such under a licensing or other regulatory regime established under any written law;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any obligation imposed under any written law or by a court to remove, block or deny access to any material; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any liability of a network service provider under the Copyright Act (Cap. 63) in respect of&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr26-ps2-p1d-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">the infringement of copyright in any work or other subject-matter in which copyright subsists; or</td></tr><tr id="pr26-ps2-p1d-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the unauthorised use of any performance, the protection period of which has not expired.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr26-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“performance” and “protection period” have the same meanings as in Part&nbsp;XII of the Copyright Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“provides access”, in relation to third-party material, means the provision of the necessary technical means by which third-party material may be accessed and includes the automatic and temporary storage of the third-party material for the purpose of providing access;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“third-party”, in relation to a network service provider, means a person over whom the provider has no effective control.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 10]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1VII-"><div class="partNo">PART VII</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1VII-he-">GENERAL</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr27-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Appointment of Controller and other officers</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>27.</strong><a name="pr27-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may appoint any person to be the Controller for the purposes of this Act.</span><a name="pr27-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller shall, subject to any general or special directions of the Minister, perform such duties as are imposed and may exercise such powers as are conferred upon him by this Act or any other written law.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr27-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller may, after consultation with the Minister, appoint by name or office such number of Deputy Controllers, Assistant Controllers and other officers as the Controller considers necessary for the purpose of assisting him in the performance of his duties and the exercise of his powers under this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr27-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller may delegate the exercise of all or any of the powers conferred or duties imposed upon him by this Act (except the power of delegation conferred by this subsection) to any officer appointed under subsection&nbsp;(3), subject to such conditions or limitations as the Controller may specify.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr27-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;In exercising any of the powers of enforcement under this Act, an authorised officer shall on demand produce to the person against whom he is acting the authority issued to him by the Controller.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr27-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller, every officer appointed under subsection&nbsp;(3) and every authorised officer shall be deemed to be a public servant for the purposes of the Penal Code (Cap. 224).<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, ss. 41 and 50]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr28-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Obligation of confidentiality</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>28.</strong><a name="pr28-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;No person shall disclose any information which has been obtained by him in the performance of his duties or the exercise of his powers under this Act, unless such disclosure is made&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">with the permission of the person from whom the information was obtained or, where the information is the confidential information of a third person, with the permission of the third person;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for the purpose of the administration or enforcement of this Act;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for the purpose of assisting any public officer or officer of any other statutory board in the investigation or prosecution of any offence under any written law; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in compliance with the requirement of any court or the provisions of any written law.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr28-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this section, the reference to a person disclosing any information includes his permitting any other person to have access to any electronic record, book, register, correspondence, information, document or other material which has been obtained by him in the performance of his duties or the exercise of his powers under this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr28-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who contravenes subsection&nbsp;(1) shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $10,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months or to both.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 48; ACRA, s. 34]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr29-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Access to computers and data</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>29.</strong><a name="pr29-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller or an authorised officer shall be entitled at any time to&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">have access to and inspect and check the operation of any computer system and any associated apparatus or material which he has reasonable cause to suspect is or has been in use in connection with any offence under this Act; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">use or caused to be used any such computer system to search any data contained in or available to such computer system.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr29-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller or an authorised officer shall be entitled to require&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person by whom or on whose behalf the Controller or authorised officer has reasonable cause to suspect the computer is or has been so used; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any person having charge of, or otherwise concerned with the operation of, the computer, apparatus or material,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">to provide him with such reasonable technical and other assistance as he may require for the purposes of subsection&nbsp;(1).</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr29-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">obstructs the lawful exercise of the powers under subsection&nbsp;(1); or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">fails to comply with a request under subsection&nbsp;(2),</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $20,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months or to both.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 53]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr30-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Production of documents, etc.</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>30.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller or an authorised officer shall, for the purposes of the execution of this Act, have power to do all or any of the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">require the production of any identification document from any person in relation to any offence under this Act;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">make such inquiry as may be necessary to ascertain whether the provisions of this Act have been complied with.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 55]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr31-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Obstruction of Controller or authorised officer</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>31.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who obstructs, impedes, assaults or interferes with the Controller or any authorised officer in the performance of his functions under this Act shall be guilty of an offence.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 54]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr32-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Offences by bodies corporate, etc.</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>32.</strong><a name="pr32-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an offence under this Act committed by a body corporate is proved&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to have been committed with the consent or connivance of an officer; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to be attributable to any neglect on his part,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">the officer as well as the body corporate shall be guilty of the offence and shall be liable to be proceeded against and punished accordingly.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr32-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the affairs of a body corporate are managed by its members, subsection&nbsp;(1) shall apply in relation to the acts and defaults of a member in connection with his functions of management as if he were a director of the body corporate.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr32-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an offence under this Act committed by a partnership is proved&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to have been committed with the consent or connivance of a partner; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to be attributable to any neglect on his part,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">the partner as well as the partnership shall be guilty of the offence and shall be liable to be proceeded against and punished accordingly.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr32-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an offence under this Act committed by an unincorporated association (other than a partnership) is proved&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to have been committed with the consent or connivance of an officer of the unincorporated association or a member of its governing body; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to be attributable to any neglect on the part of such an officer or member,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">the officer or member as well as the unincorporated association shall be guilty of the offence and shall be liable to be proceeded against and punished accordingly.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr32-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“body corporate” includes a limited liability partnership;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“officer” &nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in relation to a body corporate, means any director, partner, member of the committee of management, chief executive, manager, secretary or other similar officer of the body corporate and includes any person purporting to act in any such capacity; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in relation to an unincorporated association (other than a partnership), means the president, the secretary, or any member of the committee of the unincorporated association, or any person holding a position analogous to that of president, secretary or member of such a committee and includes any person purporting to act in any such capacity;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“partner” includes a person purporting to act as a partner.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr32-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;Regulations may provide for the application of any provision of this section, with such modifications as the Minister considers appropriate, to any body corporate or unincorporated association formed or recognised under the law of a territory outside Singapore.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 49]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr33-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">General penalties</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>33.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person guilty of an offence under this Act for which no penalty is expressly provided shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $20,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months or to both.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 56]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr34-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Consent of Public Prosecutor</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>34.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;No prosecution in respect of any offence under this Act shall be instituted except by or with the consent of the Public Prosecutor.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 57]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr35-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Jurisdiction of court</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>35.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary in the Criminal Procedure Code 2010 (Act 15 of 2010), a District Court shall have jurisdiction to try any offence under this Act and shall have power to impose the full penalty or punishment in respect of the offence.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 58]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr36-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Composition of offences</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>36.</strong><a name="pr36-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Controller may, in his discretion, compound any offence under this Act which is prescribed as being an offence which may be compounded by collecting from the person reasonably suspected of having committed the offence a sum not exceeding&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">one half of the amount of the maximum fine that is prescribed for the offence; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">$5,000,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">whichever is the lower.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr36-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;On payment of such sum of money, no further proceedings shall be taken against that person in respect of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr36-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may make regulations prescribing the offences which may be compounded.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 59]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr37-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to exempt</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>37.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, exempt, subject to such terms and conditions as he thinks fit, any person or class of persons from all or any of the provisions of this Act.<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 60]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr38-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Regulations</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>38.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may make regulations to prescribe anything which is required to be prescribed under this Act (except section&nbsp;22) and generally for the carrying out of the provisions of this Act (except section&nbsp;22).<div class="sourceNote">[ETA, s. 61]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr39-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Transitional provisions</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>39.</strong><a name="pr39-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to subsection&nbsp;(2), this Act shall apply to all acts or transactions done in relation to an electronic record, including the generation, signing or communication of an electronic record, made on or after the date of commencement of this Act.</span><a name="pr39-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;If, immediately before the date of commencement of this Act&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by virtue of section&nbsp;8 of the repealed Electronic Transactions Act (Cap.&nbsp;88, 1999 Ed.) (referred to in this section as the repealed Act), an electronic signature was treated as having satisfied a rule of law requiring a signature, or providing certain consequences if a document is not signed;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by virtue of section&nbsp;9 of the repealed Act, an electronic record was treated as having satisfied a rule of law requiring certain documents, records or information to be retained; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by virtue of section&nbsp;15 of the repealed Act, an electronic record was treated as having been despatched or received,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">the provisions of this Act shall not affect that treatment of the electronic signature or electronic record, as the case may be.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div <div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Explosive Substances Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 100)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Ordinance 6 of 1924)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2014</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(28th February 2014)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act relating to explosive substances.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[18th July 1924]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Explosive Substances Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, “explosive substance” shall be deemed to include&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any material for making any explosive substance; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any apparatus, machine, implement or material used, or intended to be used, or adapted for causing, or aiding in causing, any explosion in or with any explosive substance, and any part of any such apparatus, machine or implement.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Penalty for causing explosion likely to endanger life or property</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who unlawfully and maliciously causes by any explosive substance an explosion of a nature likely to endanger life or to cause serious injury to property shall, whether or not any injury to person or property has been actually caused, be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 10 years or to caning, or to any 2 of such punishments.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Penalty for attempt to cause explosion, or for making or keeping explosives, with intent to endanger life or property</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who unlawfully and maliciously&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">does any act with intent to cause by an explosive substance, or conspires to cause by an explosive substance, an explosion of a nature likely to endanger life or to cause serious injury to property; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">makes, or has in his possession or under his control, any explosive substance with intent by means of the explosive substance to endanger life or cause serious injury to property, or to enable any other person by means of the explosive substance to endanger life or cause serious injury to property,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">shall, whether any explosion does or does not take place and whether or not any injury to person or property has been actually caused, be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 10 years or to caning, or to any 2 of such punishments.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Penalty for making or possessing explosives under suspicious circumstances</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who makes or knowingly has in his possession or under his control any explosive substance, under such circumstances as to give rise to a reasonable suspicion that he is not making it or does not have it in his possession or under his control for a lawful object, shall, unless he can show that he made it or had it in his possession or under his control for a lawful object, be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 7 years or to caning, or to any 2 of such punishments.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Penalty for abetment</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who by the supply of or solicitation for money, the providing of premises, the supply of materials, or in any manner whatsoever, procures, counsels, aids, abets, or is accessory to, the commission of any offence under this Act shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to be punished with the punishment provided for the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="3ac0c393-f713-4584-acdd-fb0754c49e9e"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="7e6a4371-dda8-43dd-878c-e607b41acf89"></div></div>

<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Health Products Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 122D)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 15 of 2007)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2008</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1I-"><div class="partNo">PART I</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1I-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title and commencement</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table
