name="pr1-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Part&nbsp;XIV shall come into operation on such date as the Minister charged with the responsibility for national development may, by notification in the <em>Gazette</em>, appoint.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong><a name="pr2-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“active ingredient” means any substance or compound that is usable in the manufacture of a health product as a pharmacologically active constituent;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“adverse effect”, in relation to a health product, means any debilitating, harmful, toxic or detrimental effect that the health product has been found to have or to be likely to have on the body or health of humans when such health product is used by or administered to humans;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“advertisement”, in relation to a health product, means the publication, dissemination or conveyance of any information for the purpose of promoting, whether directly or indirectly, the sale or use of that health product by any means or in any form, including the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">publication in a newspaper, magazine, journal or other periodical;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">display of posters or notices;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">circulars, handbills, brochures, pamphlets, books or other documents;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">letters addressed to individuals or bodies corporate or unincorporate;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">photographs or cinematograph films;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">sound broadcasting, television, the Internet or other media;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">public demonstration of the use of the health product; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>h</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">offer of trials of the health product to members of the public;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><span id="pr2-ps1-pd-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="definitionRepealed">[<em>Deleted by Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“analyst” means any person who is designated as an analyst by the Chief Executive under section&nbsp;8;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Appeal Advisory Committee” means an Appeal Advisory Committee established by the Minister under section&nbsp;11;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Authority” means the Health Sciences Authority established under section&nbsp;3 of the Health Sciences Authority Act (Cap. 122C);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Chief Executive” means the person appointed under section&nbsp;15 of the Health Sciences Authority Act to be the Chief Executive of the Authority;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“clinical trial” means an investigation in respect of a health product that involves human subjects and that is intended to&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">discover or verify its clinical, pharmacological or pharmacodynamic effects;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">identify any adverse effect that may arise from its use;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">study its absorption, distribution, metabolism and excretion; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">ascertain its safety or efficacy;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“efficacy”, in relation to a health product that is a device, includes the ability of the device to properly carry out its intended purpose;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“enforcement officer” means&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the Chief Executive; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any officer of the Authority or any other person who is appointed by the Chief Executive under section&nbsp;7 to be an enforcement officer;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“health product” means any substance, preparation or device&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">that&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdhealthproduct-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">is represented for use by humans;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdhealthproduct-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">whether because of its presentation or otherwise, is likely to be taken for use by humans; or</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdhealthproduct-p1a-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">is included in a class of substances, preparations or devices which are or are ordinarily intended for use by humans,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1SO" style="font-size:13pt">solely or principally for a health-related purpose; and</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">that falls within any of the categories of health products specified in the First&nbsp;Schedule;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“health-related purpose” means a therapeutic, preventive, palliative, diagnostic or cosmetic purpose, or any other purpose for the promotion or preservation of human health and well-being, and includes the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">preventing, diagnosing, monitoring, treating, curing or alleviating any disease, disorder, ailment, injury, handicap or abnormal physical or mental state, or the symptoms thereof, in humans;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">compensating for any injury or handicap in humans;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">investigating, modifying or replacing any part of the human anatomy or any physiological process in humans;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">testing the susceptibility of humans to any disease, disorder or ailment;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">influencing, controlling or preventing conception in humans;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">testing for pregnancy in humans;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">inducing anaesthesia in humans;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>h</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">destroying or inhibiting micro-organisms that may be harmful to humans; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>i</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">cleansing, fragrancing, deodorising, beautifying, preserving, improving, altering or restoring the complexion, skin, hair, nails or teeth of humans;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“importer’s licence” means a licence authorising the holder thereof to import any health product;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“intended purpose”, in relation to a health product, means the use for which the health product is intended according to the specifications of its manufacturer as stated on any or all of the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the label of the health product;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the instructions for use of the health product;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the promotional materials in relation to the health product;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“label”, in relation to a health product or an active ingredient, means any written, printed or graphic representation that appears on or is attached to the health product or active ingredient or any part of its packaging, and includes any informational sheet or leaflet that accompanies the health product or active ingredient when it is being supplied;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“licence” means any licence issued by the Authority under this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“manufacture”, in relation to a health product, means to make, fabricate, produce or process the health product and includes&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any process carried out in the course of so making, fabricating, producing or processing the health product; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the packaging and labelling of the health product before it is supplied;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“manufacturer’s licence” means a licence authorising the holder thereof to manufacture any health product;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Minister” means, except in Part&nbsp;XIV, the Minister charged with the responsibility for health;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“National Parks Board” means the National Parks Board established by the repealed National Parks Act (Cap. 198A, 1991 Ed.) as in force before 1 July 1996 and continued by section 3 of the National Parks Board Act (Cap. 198A);<div class="amendNote">[Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“packaging”, in relation to a health product or an active ingredient, means the container and other packaging material in which the health product or active ingredient is supplied;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“presentation”, in relation to a health product, means the way in which the health product is presented for supply, and includes matters relating to the name of the health product, the packaging and labelling of the health product and any other informational material associated with the health product;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“prohibited substance” means a substance that is prescribed as a substance that is not to be contained at all in any health product or in any particular category of health products;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“recall”, in relation to a health product, means any action taken by its manufacturer, importer, supplier or registrant to remove the health product from the market or to retrieve the health product from any person to whom it has been supplied, because the health product&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">may be hazardous to health;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">may fail to conform to any claim made by its manufacturer or importer relating to its quality, safety or efficacy; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">may not meet the requirements of this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Register of Health Products” means the Register of Health Products kept and maintained by the Authority under section&nbsp;34;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“registered health product” means a health product currently registered under Part&nbsp;VII;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“registrant”, in relation to a registered health product, means the person who applied for and obtained the registration of the health product under this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“regulations” means regulations made under section&nbsp;72;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“sample”, in relation to a health product or an active ingredient, includes a sample of the packaging of the health product or active ingredient;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“supply”, in relation to a health product, means to transfer possession of the health product by any means whether or not for reward, and includes the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to sell the health product, whether by retail, wholesale or auction;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to expose or display the health product as an invitation to treat;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to transfer possession of the health product by exchange, gift, lease, loan, hire or hire-purchase;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to supply the health product in connection with&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdsupply-p1d-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">a contract for the provision of any goods or the performance of any service; or</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdsupply-p1d-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">any advertising, sponsorship or promotional activity;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to supply the health product by way of administration to or application in any person in the course of any diagnosis, treatment or test;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to offer, agree or attempt to supply the health product in any of the ways described in paragraphs&nbsp;(<em>a</em>) to (<em>e</em>) or to cause or permit the health product to be so supplied; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to keep or possess the health product for the purpose of supplying it in any of the ways described in paragraphs&nbsp;(<em>a</em>) to (<em>f</em>);</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“veterinarian” means a person who is licensed under section&nbsp;53 of the Animals and Birds Act (Cap. 7) to treat, vaccinate or inoculate any animal or bird;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“wholesale”, in relation to a health product, means any one or more of the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">supplying the health product to a person who obtains the health product for the purposes of supplying it again to some other person;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">supplying the health product to a person as a commercial sample in the normal course of a lawful trade;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">supplying the health product to a Government department or statutory body which requires the health product for the purposes of the public service or use in connection with the exercise of any statutory power;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">supplying the health product to a person or an institution concerned with scientific education or research which requires the health product for the purpose of education or research;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">supplying the health product to a person who requires the health product for the purpose of enabling him to comply with any requirements made by, or in pursuance of, any written law with respect to the medical treatment of persons employed by that person in any business or trade carried out by that person;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">supplying the health product to a person who requires to use the health product, other than by way of administration to one or more persons, for the purpose of his business or trade;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">supplying the health product by export to a party outside Singapore;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“wholesaler’s licence” means a licence authorising the holder thereof to supply any health product by wholesale.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr2-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this Act&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a health product is adulterated if it contains or has been mixed with any substance or ingredient that is not stated on its label as being one of its constituent substances or ingredients, except where the substance is an inactive ingredient&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">which is permitted as a food additive or flavouring agent according to the Codex Alimentarius or such other similar document as may be prescribed; or</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">which is approved by the Authority;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a health product is counterfeit if&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">it is presented in such a manner as to resemble or pass off as a registered health product when in fact it is not; or</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">it is presented with any false information as to its manufacturer or origin;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a health product is tampered with if it has been modified or interfered with in any way, including through the introduction or incorporation therein of any substance or component that is not referred to in the specifications of its manufacturer; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a health product is unwholesome if&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">it is not in conformity as regards strength, quality or purity with the specifications of its manufacturer;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">it has a strength which differs from, or a standard of purity or quality which falls below, that which is represented on its label;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">any of its constituent substances or ingredients, as stated on its label, has been extracted or omitted from it;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2iv-"><td class="p2No">(iv)</td><td class="p2Txt">it contains any prohibited substance or any substance in excess of the prescribed permitted concentration;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2v-"><td class="p2No">(v)</td><td class="p2Txt">it consists in whole or in part of any filthy, putrid or decomposed substance;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2vi-"><td class="p2No">(vi)</td><td class="p2Txt">it has been manufactured or stored under unsanitary conditions;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2vii-"><td class="p2No">(vii)</td><td class="p2Txt">it has been kept in a package which is composed in whole or in part of any substance which may render the contents injurious to health;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2viii-"><td class="p2No">(viii)</td><td class="p2Txt">it has been packed with any substance so as to reduce the purity, quality, strength or beneficial properties that it would have had if it had not been so packed; or</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps2-p1d-p2ix-"><td class="p2No">(ix)</td><td class="p2Txt">it has passed its expected useful life or its expiry date as assigned by its manufacturer.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this Act, a licence or registration is not in force during the period of its suspension.</td></tr></tbody></table></span></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Purposes of Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The purposes of this Act are&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to provide for the categorisation of health products in accordance with their different characteristics and uses;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to provide the framework for a uniform approach for&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr3-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">the registration of health products; and</td></tr><tr id="pr3-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the regulation of the manufacture, import, supply, storage, presentation and advertisement of health products;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to allow for each category of health product to be registered and regulated by reference to its formulation, composition, design specification, quality, safety and efficacy and within the framework provided by this Act; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to prescribe the standards for health products in relation to their formulation, composition, design specification, quality, safety, efficacy and presentation.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Act to apply only to health products specified in First Schedule</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Except for and as provided in Part&nbsp;XIV, this Act shall apply only in relation to the categories of health products that are specified and described in the first and second columns of the First&nbsp;Schedule to the extent prescribed in the third column thereof.</span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, after consultation with the Authority, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em> add to, amend or vary the categories and descriptions of health products in the First&nbsp;Schedule and the extent to which the provisions of this Act shall apply thereto.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;In prescribing the extent to which this Act shall apply to any category of health products, the Minister may, in the third column of the First&nbsp;Schedule, specify the provisions or any part of any provision of this Act that shall or shall not apply in relation to such category of health products.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Act not to apply to supply or use of health products and active ingredients for veterinary purposes</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as provided in Part&nbsp;XIV, this Act shall not apply in relation to the supply or use by a veterinarian of any health product or active ingredient for veterinary purposes.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1II-"><div class="partNo">PART II</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1II-he-">ADMINISTRATION</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Administration of Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Authority shall be responsible for the administration and enforcement of this Act (except for Part&nbsp;XIV) subject to the general and special directions of the Minister.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr7-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Appointment of enforcement officers</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>7.</strong><a name="pr7-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chief Executive may in writing appoint&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any officer of the Authority; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">with the approval of the Authority, any other person,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">to be an enforcement officer for the purposes of this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr7-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every enforcement officer, when exercising his powers and carrying out his duties under this Act, shall comply with such general or special directions as may, from time to time, be given to him by the Chief Executive.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr7-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every enforcement officer when exercising any of his powers under this Act shall, if not in uniform, declare his office and shall, on demand, produce to any person affected by the exercise of that power such identification card as the Authority may direct to be carried by the enforcement officer when exercising such power.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr8-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Designation of analysts</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>8.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chief Executive may designate any suitably qualified person as an analyst to carry out any test, evaluation or analysis as may be necessary for the purpose of the administration and enforcement of this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr9-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Enforcement officers and analysts deemed to be public officers</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>9.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Every enforcement officer and analyst shall be deemed to be a public servant within the meaning of the Penal Code (Cap. 224).</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr10-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Advisory Committees</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>10.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Authority may establish one or more Advisory Committees consisting of such persons as it thinks fit to appoint for the purpose of advising the Authority on such matters arising from the administration and enforcement of this Act as are referred to them by the Authority.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Appeal Advisory Committees</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may establish one or more Appeal Advisory Committees consisting of such persons as he thinks fit to appoint for the purpose of&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">assisting him in his determination of any appeal that is brought to him under this Act; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">advising him on any matter arising from any such appeal.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" <hr style="width:100%">
 <table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="PADate">The following Act was passed by Parliament on 2 October 2017 and assented to by the President on 23 October 2017:—</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="titlepg" id="aT-">Infrastructure Protection Act 2017</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="actNo">(No. 41 of 2017)</p><hr style="width:15%"><p class="sigTxtC">I assent.</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sigTbl" id="as-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sig" id="as-sg-">HALIMAH YACOB,</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="position" id="as-sp-">President.</div><div class="sigDate"> 23 October 2017.</div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="cDateL">Date of Commencement: 18 December 2018</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to provide for the protection of certain areas, places and other premises in Singapore against security risks, to repeal the Protected Areas and Protected Places Act (Chapter&nbsp;256 of the 2013&nbsp;Revised Edition) and to make consequential amendments to certain other Acts.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="enactWd" id="aw-">Be it enacted by the President with the advice and consent of the Parliament of Singapore, as follows:</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P11-"><div class="partNo">PART 1</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P11-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title and commencement</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act is the Infrastructure Protection Act 2017 and comes into operation on a date that the Minister appoints by notification in the <em>Gazette</em>.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong><a name="pr2-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“act of terrorism” means any of the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a terrorist bombing offence within the meaning of the Terrorism (Suppression of Bombings) Act (Cap.&nbsp;324A);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a terrorist act within the meaning of the Terrorism (Suppression of Financing) Act (Cap.&nbsp;325);</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Appeal Advisory Board” means the Appeal Advisory Board established under section&nbsp;63;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“approved security plan”, for a special development or a special infrastructure, means any security plan that is approved by the Commissioner and is in force for that special development or that special infrastructure under this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“authorised officer”, for a protected area or a protected place, means&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a police officer;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">an officer or a senior military expert of the Singapore Armed Forces;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a soldier of the Singapore Armed Forces who is deployed to guard that protected area or that protected place;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">an officer or a member of a visiting force lawfully present in Singapore who is deployed to guard that protected area or that protected place under the terms of any treaty, agreement or arrangement to which the Government is a party;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a prison officer (as defined in section&nbsp;2 of the Prisons Act (Cap.&nbsp;247)) who is deployed to guard that protected area or that protected place;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">an immigration officer (as defined in section&nbsp;2(1) of the Immigration Act (Cap.&nbsp;133)) who is deployed to guard that protected area or that protected place;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">an auxiliary police officer who is deployed to guard that protected area or that protected place; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>h</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a security officer who is authorised by the Commissioner of Police under section&nbsp;6(1) and is deployed to guard that protected area or that protected place;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“authority” &nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for a protected area, means the person who is designated as the authority of the protected area in the protected area order for the protected area; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for a protected place, means the person who is designated as the authority of the protected place in the protected place order for the protected place;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“auxiliary police officer” has the same meaning as in section&nbsp;2(1) of the Police Force Act (Cap.&nbsp;235);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“building” means any permanent or temporary building or structure;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Commissioner” means the Commissioner of Infrastructure Protection appointed under section&nbsp;5, and (subject to any condition or restriction imposed under that section) includes a Deputy Commissioner of Infrastructure Protection or an Assistant Commissioner of Infrastructure Protection appointed under that section;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Commissioner of Police” means the Commissioner of Police appointed under section&nbsp;6(1) of the Police Force Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“critical asset”, for any premises, means any facility, system or equipment which, if damaged or destroyed, may have a debilitating impact on the functioning of the premises;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“document” has the same meaning as in section&nbsp;29 of the Penal Code (Cap.&nbsp;224);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“major renovation”, for any premises, means&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in the case of any part of a building that contains a critical asset, or is a public place or is otherwise accessible to vehicles or vessels, any alteration, extension, repair, dismantling or demolition works carried out to the structure or glazing of that part;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any installation or relocation of a critical asset in the premises; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any alteration, extension, dismantling or demolition works affecting the perimeter of the premises;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“member of a state force” means any of the following persons:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a police officer;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">an auxiliary police officer;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">an officer, a senior military expert or a soldier of the Singapore Armed Forces;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a member of the Singapore Civil Defence Force, as defined in section&nbsp;2 of the Civil Defence Act (Cap.&nbsp;42);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any public officer, or any officer in a class of public officers, authorised in writing by the Minister for the purposes of Part&nbsp;6;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“new development” means any new development that is proposed to be or being constructed;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“occupier”, for any premises, means the person in occupation or having the charge, management or control of the premises;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“officer”, “senior military expert”, “serviceman” and “soldier”, in relation to the Singapore Armed Forces, have the same meanings as in section&nbsp;2(1) of the Singapore Armed Forces Act (Cap.&nbsp;295);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“owner” &nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for the common property of a building erected on land comprised in a strata title plan, means the management corporation having control of the building;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for the limited common property of a building erected on land comprised in a strata title plan, means the subsidiary management corporation having control of that limited common property;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for the common property of a building comprising flats sold under Part&nbsp;IV of the Housing and Development Act (Cap.&nbsp;129), means&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdowner-p1c-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">in the case where a Town Council (established under the Town Councils Act (Cap.&nbsp;329A)) is liable for the management of that common property, the Town Council; and</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdowner-p1c-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">in any other case, the Housing and Development Board (established under the Housing and Development Act); and</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for any other premises, includes any mortgagee in possession and any person for the time being receiving the rent for the premises whether on the person’s own account or as agent or trustee or as receiver, or who would receive the same if the premises were let to a tenant, and any person whose name is entered in the Valuation List prepared under section&nbsp;10 of the Property Tax Act (Cap.&nbsp;254) as the owner of the premises;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“personal property”, in relation to a person, means any thing worn or carried by the person or apparently in the immediate control of the person;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“police officer” has the same meaning as in section&nbsp;2(1) of the Police Force Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“premises” includes&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any building;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any land, whether built on or not;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any body of water; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any area or place, whether or not enclosed, and whether underground or underwater;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“protected area” means any premises in Singapore declared in a protected area order to be a protected area;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“protected area order” means an order made under section&nbsp;8 declaring any premises to be a protected area, and includes the order as amended under section&nbsp;11;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“protected infrastructure” means&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a protected area;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a protected place;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a special development;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a special infrastructure; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any premises in respect of which a security directive under section&nbsp;55 or a Minister’s order under section&nbsp;58 is issued;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“protected place” means any premises in Singapore declared in a protected place order to be a protected place;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“protected place order” means an order made under section&nbsp;14 declaring any premises to be a protected place, and includes the order as amended under section&nbsp;17;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“public place” means any premises to which the public, or a section of the public, ordinarily has access, whether on payment, by invitation, as of right, or by express or implied permission;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“repealed Act” means the Protected Areas and Protected Places Act (Cap.&nbsp;256, 2013&nbsp;Ed.) repealed by this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“responsible person”, for a special development or a special infrastructure, has the meaning given to that expression in section&nbsp;32;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“security agency” means any person licensed as a security agency under the Private Security Industry Act (Cap.&nbsp;250A);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“security measure” includes any installation, equipment, works, action or procedure manufactured, used or designed to be used for the purposes of reducing a security risk;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“security officer” has the same meaning as in section&nbsp;13 of the Private Security Industry Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Singapore Armed Forces” has the same meaning as in section&nbsp;2(1) of the Singapore Armed Forces Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“special development” means a new development designated as a special development under section&nbsp;34;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“special infrastructure” means&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a special infrastructure described in section&nbsp;40; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any premises designated as a special infrastructure under section&nbsp;41;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“specified surrounding area”, for a protected area or a protected place, means any surrounding area of that protected area or that protected place that is specified in the protected area order (for that protected area) or the protected place order (for that protected place) for the purposes of sections&nbsp;27 and 28;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“specified works” &nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for a special development, means any works for or affecting the foundation, retaining structure, substructure or superstructure of any building to be or being constructed under the special development; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for a special infrastructure, means&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdspecifiedworks-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">any extension of the special infrastructure;</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdspecifiedworks-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">any major renovation to the special infrastructure; or</td></tr><tr id="pr2-ps1-pdspecifiedworks-p1b-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">any other type of works prescribed by the Minister;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“temporary occupation permit”, for a special development or a special infrastructure, means a temporary occupation permit granted or a certificate of statutory completion issued under the Building Control Act (Cap.&nbsp;29) for that special development or that special infrastructure;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“vehicle” means any vehicle whether mechanically propelled or otherwise;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“vessel” includes any ship, boat, craft (including submersible craft), floating platform or air‑cushioned vehicle, whether mechanically propelled or otherwise, that is used to navigate any body of water;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“visiting force” has the same meaning as in section&nbsp;2(1) of the Visiting Forces Act (Cap.&nbsp;344).</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr2-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires, a reference to any premises, building or protected infrastructure includes a reference to a part of the premises, building or protected infrastructure.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Application of this Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong><a name="pr3-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as provided in subsection&nbsp;(2), this Act binds the Government and applies to any premises owned or occupied by the Government.</span><a name="pr3-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Act renders the Government liable to prosecution for an offence.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, no person is immune from prosecution for any offence under this Act by reason only that the person is an employee of or is engaged to provide services to the Government.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Operation of other written laws</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Act affects the operation of, or derogates from, the following written laws:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Air Navigation Act (Cap.&nbsp;6);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Building Control Act (Cap.&nbsp;29);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Civil Defence Shelter Act (Cap.&nbsp;42A);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Criminal Procedure Code (Cap.&nbsp;68);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Fire Safety Act (Cap.&nbsp;109A);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Liquor Control (Supply and Consumption) Act&nbsp;2015 (Act&nbsp;5 of 2015);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>g</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Planning Act (Cap.&nbsp;232);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>h</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Police Force Act (Cap.&nbsp;235);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>i</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Private Security Industry Act (Cap.&nbsp;250A);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>j</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Public Order Act (Cap.&nbsp;257A);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>k</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Singapore Armed Forces Act (Cap.&nbsp;295);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>l</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any other prescribed written law (or any part of that written law as prescribed).</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, nothing in this Act affects&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the exercise by a police officer or an auxiliary police officer of any power under the Criminal Procedure Code, the Public Order Act or any other written law; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the exercise by a serviceman of any power in accordance with section&nbsp;201D of the Singapore Armed Forces Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="f207986b-d662-43e6-aa8e-b195b1cb711f"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="537d1a5c-ebdb-4ed3-a8fe-0377f4a1300a"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" <div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Inland Revenue Authority of Singapore Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 138A)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 25 of 1992)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2012</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(31st October 2012)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to establish and incorporate the Inland Revenue Authority of Singapore, to provide for its functions and powers, and for matters connected therewith.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[1st September 1992]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1I-"><div class="partNo">PART I</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1I-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Inland Revenue Authority of Singapore Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Authority” means the Inland Revenue Authority of Singapore established under section&nbsp;3;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Chairman” means the Chairman of the Authority and includes any temporary Chairman of the Authority;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“chief executive officer” means the chief executive officer of the Authority and includes any person acting in that capacity;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Deputy Chairman” means the Deputy Chairman of the Authority and includes any temporary Deputy Chairman of the Authority;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“member” means a member of the Authority.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="b3f4fc64-6e07-47b4-b985-137443a76925"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="e586633d-5842-46f4-a3c0-60d04f973e7d"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="ccef35b5-a03c-4f1f-8d5c-a61d9c88f934"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="4188b419-c41a-4dc7-800b-2777fc26bcff"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="a472793b-28ff-48e1-991d-1b50e552147e"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="168903b6-7324-49e9-962c-b5a0cf946fbd"></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="815606a2-f62a-4068-931c-7cc3d2c6c4c0"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="b23d0406-053b-46f0-afb5-f06067f4a9e2"></div><div class="dms" <div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Judges’ Remuneration Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 147)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 7 of 1994)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 1995</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(15th March 1995)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to provide for the remuneration of the Judges of the Supreme Court.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[1st September 1994]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Judges’ Remuneration Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1A.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires —<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“annual pensionable salary”, in relation to a holder of any judicial office, means the emoluments of the holder, the whole or any part of which count&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for a pension in accordance with the Pensions Act (Cap.&nbsp;225) if the holder is appointed to any judicial office before the date of commencement of the Judges’ Remuneration (Amendment) Act 2014; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for a gratuity in accordance with this Act if the holder is first appointed to any judicial office on or after that date;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“judicial office” means the office of the Chief Justice, a Judge of Appeal or a Judge of the High Court.<div class="amendNote">[Act 38 of 2014 wef 01/01/2015]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Remuneration of Judges</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong><a name="pr2-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall be paid to the Chief Justice, every Judge of Appeal and every other Judge of the Supreme Court such annual pensionable salaries as the Minister may, from time to time by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, determine.</span><a name="pr2-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;A Judge of the Supreme Court shall receive, in addition to his salary, such pensionable and non-pensionable allowances and privileges as the Minister may determine, which shall not be less than such pensionable and non-pensionable allowances and privileges as a public officer receiving the same pensionable salary would receive.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any salary or allowance payable to a Judge of the Supreme Court under this section shall&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">commence from the date of appointment, but subject to the fulfilment of any condition on which the allowance is payable;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">accrue from day to day; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">be payable monthly on the last day of each month or on such other day in each month as the Minister for Finance may from time to time determine.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any order made under subsection&nbsp;(1) shall be presented to Parliament as soon as possible after publication in the <em>Gazette</em>.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Savings</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong><a name="pr3-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2(2)(<em>b</em>) of the repealed Judges’ Remuneration Act (Cap. 147, 1985 Ed.) shall continue to apply to a Judge of the Supreme Court appointed before 1st September 1994.</span><a name="pr3-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The annual pensionable salary of a Judge of Appeal from 1st July 1993 to the day immediately before 1st September 1994 shall be $253,200.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Gratuity upon retirement or death in harness</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;An individual —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">who holds a judicial office; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">who retires from that office on attaining 65&nbsp;years of age or in such other circumstances as may be prescribed,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">may, on retirement, be granted by the President, in respect of each complete month of the individual’s reckonable service which is unbroken, a gratuity determined in accordance with a rate prescribed in regulations subject to such limit as may be prescribed in those regulations.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where at any time after the date of commencement of the Judges’ Remuneration (Amendment) Act 2014, an individual dies while holding any judicial office, there may be paid to such of the deceased’s dependants as the President may think fit or, if there are no dependants, to the legal personal representatives of the deceased, a death gratuity determined in accordance with regulations.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;It shall be lawful for the President to make regulations for the granting of gratuities to individuals who have held judicial office or to their legal personal representatives or dependants, and for such other matters as may be necessary or expedient to give effect to this section.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;A gratuity granted under this section —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is not assignable or transferable, except for the purpose of satisfying —<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr4-ps4-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">a debt due to the Government; or</td></tr><tr id="pr4-ps4-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">an order of any court for the payment of periodical sums of money towards the maintenance of the spouse or former spouse or minor child, whether legitimate or not, of the individual to whom the gratuity has been granted; and</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is not liable to be attached, sequestered or levied upon for or in respect of any debt or claim except a debt due to the Government.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, no holder of a judicial office shall have an absolute right to compensation for past services or to any gratuity under this section.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall be charged on and paid out of the Consolidated Fund all sums of money as may from time to time be granted by way of gratuity or death gratuity in accordance with this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section, “reckonable service” means —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">service in one or more judicial offices;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">service as a Judicial Commissioner of the Supreme Court if, and only if, it immediately precedes appointment to a judicial office without any break; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">such other service in the Government (except as a Senior Judge or an International Judge of the Supreme Court) that regulations under this section prescribe to be reckonable for the purposes of a gratuity or death gratuity under this section, if, and only if, that other service immediately precedes appointment to a judicial office without any break.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps8-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(8)&nbsp;&nbsp;This section applies only to an individual who is first appointed to any judicial office on or after the date of commencement of the Judges’ Remuneration (Amendment) Act 2014.<div class="amendNote">[Act 38 of 2014 wef 01/01/2015]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="tail"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="LH" id="xv-"><p class="LHHdrNoBold">LEGISLATIVE HISTORY</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="LHHdrNoBold">Judges’ Remuneration Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="LHHdrNoBold">(CHAPTER
