<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Maintenance of Religious Harmony Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 167A)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 26 of 1990)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2001</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(31st July 2001)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to provide for the maintenance of religious harmony and for establishing a Presidential Council for Religious Harmony and for matters connected therewith.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[31st March 1992]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1I-"><div class="partNo">PART I</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1I-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Maintenance of Religious Harmony Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Council” means the Presidential Council for Religious Harmony constituted under section&nbsp;3;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Presidential Council for Minority Rights” means the Presidential Council for Minority Rights constituted under Part&nbsp;VII of the Constitution of the Republic of Singapore;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“publication” includes any newsletter, journal, periodical, book, film, videotape, audio tape or any written, pictorial, aural or printed matter containing any audio or visible representation which by its images, form, shape or sound or in any other manner is capable of suggesting words or ideas, and every copy and reproduction or substantial reproduction of any publication;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“religious institution” includes a church, cathedral, chapel, sanctuary, mosque, surau, temple, synagogue or other place of worship;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“religious group” includes&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any company or other body corporate incorporated under the Companies Act (Cap. 50) or any other written law for the purpose of promoting any religion, religious worship or dealing with religious affairs or practising, conducting, teaching or propagating any religious belief; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any body of persons, whether or not registered as a society under the Societies Act (Cap. 311), whose object is the promotion of any religion, religious worship or the practice, conduct, teaching or propagating of any religious belief.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1II-"><div class="partNo">PART II</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1II-he-">ESTABLISHMENT OF PRESIDENTIAL COUNCIL FOR RELIGIOUS HARMONY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Establishment of Council</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong><a name="pr3-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall be a Presidential Council for Religious Harmony comprising a chairman and not less than 6 and not more than 15 other members.</span><a name="pr3-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Not less than two-thirds of the members of the Council shall be representatives of the major religions in Singapore and the other members shall be persons who, in the opinion of the Presidential Council for Minority Rights, have distinguished themselves in public service or community relations in Singapore.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The chairman and every member of the Council shall be appointed by the President, on the advice of the Presidential Council for Minority Rights, for a period of 3 years all of whom shall be eligible for reappointment.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding subsection&nbsp;(3), a member, other than the chairman, may be appointed for any shorter period of not less than one year.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;The President may, after consultation with the Presidential Council for Minority Rights, at any time revoke the appointment of the chairman or any member of the Council and may, on the advice of the Presidential Council for Minority Rights, appoint any person to fill any vacancy which may arise in the Council for any reason whatsoever.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;The President may, acting in his discretion, refuse to appoint any person as chairman or member of the Council or to revoke any such appointment if he does not concur with the advice or recommendation of the Council. <div class="amendNote">[11/91]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&nbsp;&nbsp;No person shall be qualified to be appointed as a member of the Council unless he is&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a citizen of Singapore;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">not less than 35 years of age;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">resident in Singapore; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">not liable to any of the disqualifications provided in subsection&nbsp;(8).</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps8-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(8)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person shall be disqualified for appointment as a member of the Council who&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is mentally disordered and incapable of managing himself or his affairs;<div class="amendNote">[21/2008 wef 01/03/2010]</div></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is insolvent or an undischarged bankrupt;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">has been convicted of an offence by a court in Singapore or Malaysia and sentenced to imprisonment for a term of not less than one year or to a fine of not less than $2,000 and has not received a free pardon, except that where the conviction is by a court in Malaysia, the person shall not be so disqualified unless the offence is also one which, had it been committed in Singapore, would have been punishable by a court in Singapore; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">has voluntarily acquired the citizenship of, or exercised the rights of citizenship in, a foreign country or has made a declaration of allegiance to a foreign country.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps9-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(9)&nbsp;&nbsp;A member shall vacate his seat in the Council if&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">he ceases to be a citizen of Singapore;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by writing under his hand addressed to the chairman he resigns his seat; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">he becomes subject to any of the disqualifications provided in subsection&nbsp;(8).</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Functions of Council</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The functions of the Council shall be&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to consider and report to the Minister on matters affecting the maintenance of religious harmony in Singapore which are referred to the Council by the Minister or by Parliament; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to consider and make recommendations on orders referred to the Council by the Minister under section&nbsp;11.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Council shall have the power to appoint a Secretary to the Council and such other officers as may be required to enable the Council to carry out its functions under this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Council may, subject to the provisions of this Act, regulate its own procedure.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Council shall not transact any business unless a quorum of not less than half of its members, including the chairman or member presiding, is present.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;The chairman, if present, shall preside at all meetings of the Council.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;Whenever the office of chairman is vacant or the chairman for any reason is unable to attend a meeting, such other member as the members present shall elect shall preside at the meeting.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Validity of Council’s actions</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong><a name="pr5-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Council may, subject to section&nbsp;4(4), transact its business notwithstanding any vacancy among its members.</span><a name="pr5-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The proceedings or any decision of the Council shall be valid notwithstanding any defect in the appointment of its members or that some person who was not entitled to do so took part in its proceedings.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Members are public servants and protected from legal action</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong><a name="pr6-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every member or officer of the Council shall be deemed to be a public servant within the meaning of the Penal Code (Cap.&nbsp;224).</span><a name="pr6-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing done by any member or officer of the Council in good faith and in the discharge of the powers and functions of the Council shall render him liable to any suit or action.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr7-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Secrecy</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>7.</strong><a name="pr7-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as provided under section&nbsp;15, the proceedings of the Council shall be secret.</span><a name="pr7-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;No member or officer of the Council shall disclose or divulge to any person, other than the President, the Minister, the Secretary or any member of the Council, any matter which has arisen at any meeting of the Council unless he is expressly authorised to do so by the Minister.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" <div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Merchant Shipping <br>(Civil Liability and Compensation for Bunker Oil Pollution) Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 179A)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 24 of 2008)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2010</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(1st January 2010)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to give effect to the International Convention on Civil Liability for Bunker Oil Pollution Damage 2001 and to make provisions generally for matters connected therewith.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[21st November 2008]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1I-"><div class="partNo">PART I</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1I-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Merchant Shipping (Civil Liability and Compensation for Bunker Oil Pollution) Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong><a name="pr2-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Authority” means the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore established under the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore Act (Cap. 170A);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Bunker Convention” means the International Convention on Civil Liability for Bunker Oil Pollution Damage 2001;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Bunker Convention country” means a country in respect of which the Bunker Convention is in force;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Bunker Convention State” means a State which is a party to the Bunker Convention;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“bunker oil” means any hydrocarbon mineral oil, including lubricating oil, used or intended to be used for the operation or propulsion of a ship, and any residues of such oil;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Court” means the High Court;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“damage” includes loss;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Director” means the Director of Marine appointed under section&nbsp;4 of the Merchant Shipping Act (Cap. 179) and includes the Deputy Director of Marine appointed thereunder;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“gross tonnage”, in relation to a ship, means its gross tonnage calculated in accordance with the regulations in Annex 1 of the International Convention on Tonnage Measurement of Ships 1969;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“master” includes every person, except a pilot, having command or charge of a ship;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“offshore facility” has the same meaning as in the Bunker Convention;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“owner”, in relation to a ship, means the owner, and includes the registered owner, bareboat charterer, manager and operator of the ship;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“port” has the same meaning as in the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“registered owner”, in relation to a ship, means the person registered as the owner of the ship, or, in the absence of registration, the person owning the ship, except that, in relation to a ship owned by a State which is operated by a person registered in that State as the ship’s operator, it means the person registered as its operator;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“ship” means any sea-going vessel and seaborne craft of any type;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Singapore ship” has the same meaning as in the Merchant Shipping Act (Cap. 179).</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr2-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this Act&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">references to the territory of Singapore include the territorial sea and exclusive economic zone of Singapore and references to the territory of any other country include the territorial sea and exclusive economic zone of that country;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">references to the exclusive economic zone of a country are references to the exclusive economic zone of that country established in accordance with international law or, if such a zone has not been established, such area adjacent to the territorial sea of that country and extending not more than 200 nautical miles from the baselines from which the breadth of that sea is measured;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">references to a discharge or an escape of bunker oil from a ship are references to such a discharge or an escape wherever it may occur of bunker oil on board or originating from that ship;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where more than one discharge or escape results from the same occurrence or from a series of occurrences having the same origin, they shall be treated as one; but any measures taken after the first of them shall be deemed to have been taken after the discharge or escape; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where a relevant threat of contamination referred to in section&nbsp;3(2) results from a series of occurrences having the same origin, they shall be treated as a single occurrence.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Act applies in relation to&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any occurrence before 21st November 2008; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any occurrence in a series of occurrences having the same origin, if the first took place before that date.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="ddf91f83-8dc1-4078-9e8d-715094f13c04"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="003f066c-f4b2-4f46-a3e2-ef10a535f10b"></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="a08c26f8-852e-4cdf-87a4-d4a104cecd3f"></div></div>
<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">National Council of Social Service Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 195A)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 14 of 1992)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2001</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(31st July 2001)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to establish the National Council of Social Service, and for matters connected therewith.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[1st May 1992]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1I-"><div class="partNo">PART I</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1I-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the National Council of Social Service Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Board” means the Board of the Council;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Board member” means any person appointed or elected to the Board under section&nbsp;5(1);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Chairman” means the Chairman of the Community Chest;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Chief Executive Officer” means the Chief Executive Officer of the Council appointed under section&nbsp;22(1) and includes any individual acting in that capacity;<div class="amendNote">[Act 5 of 2018 wef 01/04/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Community Chest” means the Community Chest established under section&nbsp;13(1);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Council” means the National Council of Social Service established under section&nbsp;3;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Council member” means any organisation or person granted membership of the Council under section&nbsp;15;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Endowment Fund” means the Endowment Fund established under section&nbsp;12(1);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“General Fund” means the General Fund established under section&nbsp;24(1);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“President” means the President of the Board;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Vice-President” means the Vice-President of the Board.<div class="amendNote">[23/2000]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="17fca180-7091-4987-8ec1-47866bafe3c0"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="3cc5808c-28ed-4b3e-b2bd-7195e879b86b"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="ce2f7866-566b-4a7c-8731-faca0676c0f9"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="515d571a-8243-4edf-ae6d-9f846166f95f"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="df292315-24e5-4b84-b79b-97b7403c05cc"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="e54a2b4f-64c1-4507-bd68-d04b8ad1b23d"></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="25171b81-e226-47a7-a491-723541cdcf61"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="c57bb822-c667-4c19-87cd-3b8bd7ff6406"></div></div>
<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Parking Places (Surcharge) Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 215)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 26 of 1975)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2014</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(30th April 2014)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to provide for the imposition of surcharge on parking places.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[15th October 1975]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Parking Places (Surcharge) Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“designated area” means any area or place which the Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, specify as being a designated area for the purposes of this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“motor vehicle” means a mechanically propelled vehicle intended or adapted for use on roads;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“parking lot” means the space marked out in a parking place for the parking of one motor vehicle;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“parking place” means any land or premises or any part of such land or premises owned by any person, statutory board or institution and used for the parking of 5 or more motor vehicles;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Superintendent” means the Superintendent of Car Parks or a Deputy or an Assistant Superintendent of Car Parks appointed under the Parking Places Act (Cap. 214);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“surcharge” means a surcharge imposed in respect of any parking place.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Levy of surcharge</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong><a name="pr3-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall be levied a surcharge in respect of every parking place in any designated area at such rate or rates as the Minister may, from time to time, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, determine.</span><a name="pr3-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Such rate or rates shall be on the basis of the number of parking lots or otherwise as the Minister may determine.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The surcharge shall be payable at such time and in such manner as the Minister may, by order published in the <em>Gazette</em>, determine.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;The surcharge shall be payable, without demand, at the office of the Superintendent or other prescribed place.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;All surcharges required to be paid under this Act or any order made under this Act shall be recoverable as a debt due to the Government.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding the provisions of any other written law, no refund of any surcharge shall be made by the Superintendent except in such special circumstances as may be approved by him.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to seek information</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of enforcing the provisions of this Act, the Superintendent may, and as often as he thinks necessary, require any person&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to submit or render to him, within such period as he thinks fit, any form, return or information; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to answer any question raised by the Superintendent.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;All forms and returns under this Act shall be in such form as the Superintendent may require.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who fails to submit any form or return as required under subsection&nbsp;(1), or who in any such form or return makes any statement which is false in any material particular, shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $5,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to compound offences</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Superintendent may accept from any person who is reasonably suspected of having committed an offence under this Act or any of its orders or rules a sum of money not exceeding $500 by way of composition for the offence which may have been committed.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Surcharges to be paid into Consolidated Fund</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;All surcharges collected by the Superintendent shall be paid into the Consolidated Fund.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr7-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Exemption</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>7.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may exempt any parking place or such part of any parking place from all or any of the provisions of this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr8-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Non-application</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>8.</strong><a name="pr8-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The provisions of this Act  shall not apply to private parking places used exclusively in connection with any private dwelling-house for the housing or parking of vehicles kept for private use only. <div class="amendNote">[Act 24 of 2018 wef 01/05/2018]</div></span><a name="pr8-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of this section, “dwelling-house” means any building or tenement, or any part thereof, which is used, constructed or adapted for use for human habitation.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr9-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Rules</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>9.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may make rules for the purpose of carrying into effect any of the provisions of this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="tail"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="LH" id="xv-"><p class="LHHdrNoBold">LEGISLATIVE HISTORY</p><table <div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Penal Code</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 224)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Ordinance 4 of 1871)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 2008</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(30th November 2008)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to consolidate the law relating to criminal offences.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[16th September 1872]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="P4I_1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr"><div style="">Chapter I</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" style="text-transform:uppercase;">Preliminary</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act shall be called the Penal Code.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Punishment of offences committed within Singapore</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Every person shall be liable to punishment under this Code and not otherwise for every act or omission contrary to the provisions thereof, of which he is guilty within Singapore.<div class="sourceNote">[Indian PC 1860, s. 2]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Punishment of offences committed beyond, but which by law may be tried within Singapore</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person liable by law to be tried for an offence committed beyond the limits of Singapore, shall be dealt with according to the provisions of this Code for any act committed beyond Singapore, in the same manner as if such act had been committed within Singapore.<div class="sourceNote">[Indian PC 1860, s. 3]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Jurisdiction over public servants for offences committed outside Singapore</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Every public servant who, being a citizen or a permanent resident of Singapore, when acting or purporting to act in the course of his employment, commits an act or omission outside Singapore that if committed in Singapore would constitute an offence under the law in force in Singapore, is deemed to have committed that act or omission in Singapore.<div class="amendNote">[51/2007]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Offences against State and genocide committed outside Singapore by citizen or permanent resident</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4A.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Every person who, being a citizen or permanent resident of Singapore, commits an act or omission outside Singapore that if committed in Singapore would constitute an offence under Chapter&nbsp;VI (Offences against the State) or VIB (Genocide), is deemed to have committed that act or omission in Singapore.<div class="amendNote">[Act 15 of 2019 wef 01/01/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4B-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Punishment of specified offences with elements occurring in Singapore but others occurring outside Singapore</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4B.</strong><a name="pr4B-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;A specified offence is deemed to have been committed in Singapore where&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a relevant act of the specified offence occurs in Singapore and any other relevant act of that specified offence occurs outside Singapore;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a relevant act of the specified offence occurs partly in Singapore and partly outside Singapore, whether or not other relevant acts of that specified offence occur in Singapore; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the specified offence involved an intention to make a gain or cause a loss or exposure to a risk of loss or to cause harm to any person in body, mind, reputation or property, and that gain, loss or harm occurs in Singapore.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr4B-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“relevant act”, in relation to a specified offence, means an act or omission (whether occurring wholly or partly in or outside Singapore) which is a physical element of the specified offence;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“specified offence” means an offence specified in the Schedule and includes an attempt to commit the offence, an abetment of the offence and a criminal conspiracy to commit the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4B-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order in the <em>Gazette</em>, amend the Schedule.<div class="amendNote">[Act 15 of 2019 wef 01/01/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Certain laws not to be affected by this Code</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Code is intended to repeal, vary, suspend, or affect any of the provisions of any Act for punishing mutiny and desertion of officers or servicemen in the Singapore Armed Forces, or of any other law for the time being in force.<div class="sourceNote">[Indian PC 1860, s. 5]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="ae853be8-8134-41ea-a5d8-57c7b1b9e01a"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="d1856651-508d-4ddd-b31e-3bc14fb86446"></div><div class="dms" <div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Prevention of Pollution of the Sea Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 243)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 18 of 1990)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 1999</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(30th December 1999)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to give effect to the International Convention for the Prevention of Pollution from Ships 1973 as modified and added to by the Protocol of 1978, the International Convention for the Control and Management of Ships’ Ballast Water and Sediments&nbsp;2004, and to other international agreements relating to the protection of the marine environment and to the prevention, reduction and control of pollution of the sea and pollution from ships; to make provisions generally for the protection of the marine environment and for the prevention, reduction and control of pollution of the sea and pollution from ships, and for matters related thereto.<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[1st February 1991]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P1I-"><div class="partNo">PART I</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P1I-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Prevention of Pollution of the Sea Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong><a name="pr2-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“appointed authority” means the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore established under the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore Act (Cap. 170A) and any person appointed by the Minister for the purposes of this Act or any regulations made thereunder;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Authority” means the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore established under the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“ballast tank” means any tank, hold or space used for the carriage of ballast water;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“ballast water” means water with its suspended matter taken on board a ship to control trim, list, draught, stability or stresses of the ship;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“ballast water management” means mechanical, physical, chemical, and biological processes, either singularly or in combination, to remove, render harmless, or avoid the uptake or discharge of harmful aquatic organisms and pathogens within ballast water and sediments;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Ballast Water Management Convention” means the International Convention for the Control and Management of Ships’ Ballast Water and Sediments&nbsp;2004;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“ballast water management system” &nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">means any system which processes ballast water such that it meets or exceeds the ballast water performance standard in the Ballast Water Management Convention; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">includes ballast water treatment equipment, all associated control equipment, piping arrangements specified by the manufacturer of the ballast water management system as forming part of the ballast water management system, control and monitoring equipment and sampling facilities; but</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">does not include any of the ship’s ballast water fittings, such as piping, valves and pumps, that would be required to be fitted even if the ballast water management system was not fitted;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Convention” means the Convention of 1973 as modified and added to by the Protocol of 1978;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Convention of 1973” means the International Convention for the Prevention of Pollution from Ships (including its protocols, annexes and appendices) which constitutes attachment 1 to the final act of the International Conference on Marine Pollution signed in London on 2nd November 1973;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Director” means the Director of Marine appointed under section&nbsp;4 of the Merchant Shipping Act (Cap. 179) and includes the Deputy Director of Marine appointed under that section;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“discharge”, in relation to harmful substances or effluents containing such substances, means any release howsoever caused from a ship, place or thing and includes any escape, disposal, spilling, leaking, pumping, emitting or emptying but does not include&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">release of harmful substances directly arising from the exploration, exploitation and associated off-shore processing of sea-bed mineral resources; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">release of harmful substances for purposes of legitimate scientific research into pollution abatement or control;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“garbage” means all kinds of victual, domestic and operational waste excluding fresh fish and parts thereof, generated during the normal operation of the ship and liable to be disposed of continuously or periodically except sewage originating from ships;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“harmful aquatic organisms and pathogens” means aquatic organisms or pathogens which, if introduced into the sea including estuaries, or into fresh water courses, may create hazards to the environment, human health, property or resources, impair biological diversity or interfere with other legitimate uses of such areas;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“harmful substance” means any substance which, if introduced into the sea, is liable to create hazards to human health, to harm living resources and marine life, to damage amenities or to interfere with other legitimate uses of the sea, and includes any substance subject to control under this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“inspector” means a person who&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">is a surveyor of ships; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">is appointed in writing by the Director to be an inspector for the purposes of this Act or any regulations made thereunder;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“in packaged form” means in an individual package or receptacle including a freight container or a portable tank or tank container or tank vehicle or shipborne barge or other cargo unit containing harmful substances for shipment;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“marine pollutant” means a substance which is identified as a marine pollutant in the International Maritime Dangerous Goods Code published by the International Maritime Organisation, as amended from time to time;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“MARPOL” refers to the Convention;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“MARPOL surveyor” means a surveyor appointed or registered by the Director or by or on behalf of the government of a state party to the Convention;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“master” includes every person, except a pilot, having command or charge of any ship;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“noxious liquid substance” means any substance which is prescribed by regulations as being a noxious liquid substance and which is subject to the provisions of Annex II of the Convention;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“occupier”, in relation to any place on land if it has no actual occupier, means the owner thereof and, in relation to a railway wagon or road vehicle, means the person in charge of the wagon or vehicle and not the occupier of the land on which the wagon or vehicle stands;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“oil” means petroleum in any form including crude oil, fuel oil, sludge, oil refuse and refined products (other than petrochemicals which are prescribed by regulations as being subject to the provisions of Annex II of the Convention) and, without limiting the generality of the foregoing, includes the substances prescribed by regulations as being listed in Appendix I of Annex I of the Convention;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“oily mixture” means a mixture with an oil content of 15 parts or more in 1 million parts of the mixture;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“oil residues” means any waste material consisting of, or arising from, oil or oily mixture;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“oil terminal” means any place having permanent means of loading or discharging oil, whether in bulk or package, into or from any ship;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“owner”, in relation to a ship, means the person registered as the owner of the ship or, in the absence of registration, the person owning the ship or the bareboat charterer of the ship; and, in the case of a ship owned by a state and operated by a company which in that state is registered as the ship’s operator, “owner” shall include such state;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“place on land” includes anything resting on the bed or shore of the sea, or of Singapore waters, and also includes anything afloat (other than a ship) if it is anchored or attached to the bed or shore of the sea or of Singapore waters;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“plastics” includes, but is not limited to, synthetic ropes, synthetic fishing nets and plastic garbage bags;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“port” has the same meaning as in the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore Act (Cap. 170A);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Port Master” means the Port Master appointed under section&nbsp;15 of the Maritime and Port Authority of Singapore Act and includes any Deputy Port Master appointed under that section;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Protocol of 1978” means the Protocol relating to the Convention of 1973 which constitutes attachment 2 to the final act of the International Conference on Tanker Safety and Pollution Prevention signed in London on 17th February 1978;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“reception facilities” means facilities which enable ships to&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">discharge or deposit residues and mixtures, which residues and mixtures contain oil or noxious liquid substances; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">discharge sediments;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“sediments” means matter settled out of ballast water within a ship;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“ship” means a vessel of any type operating in the marine environment and includes hydrofoil boats, air cushion vehicles, submersibles, floating craft and fixed or floating platforms;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Singapore ship” means a ship registered under Part&nbsp;II of the Merchant Shipping Act (Cap. 179);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Singapore waters” means the following waters:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the whole of the sea within the seaward limits of the territorial waters of Singapore; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">all other waters (including inland waters) which are within these limits and are subject to the ebb and flow of the ordinary tides;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“surveyor of ships” means a surveyor of ships appointed under section&nbsp;5 of the Merchant Shipping Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“tank” means an enclosed space which is formed by the permanent structure of a ship and which is designed for the carriage of liquid in bulk;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“terminal” means any terminal (including an oil terminal), jetty, pier or mono-buoy and a yard or drydock (including the precincts of the terminal) in which&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">vessels are constructed, reconstructed, repaired, refitted, finished or broken up; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">ballast tanks of vessels are cleaned or repaired;<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“terminal operator” means a person or body of persons having the management of a terminal in Singapore;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“trade effluent” means the solid or liquid waste of any trade, business or manufacture.<div class="amendNote">[7/96; 8/99]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr2-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purpose of any provision of this Act relating to the discharge of oil, oily mixture, refuse, garbage, waste matter, plastics, marine pollutant in packaged form, noxious liquid substance, trade effluent, ballast water or sediments from a ship, any floating craft other than a ship which is attached to a ship shall be treated as part of the ship.<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a reference in this Act to the discharge of any oil, oily mixture, noxious liquid substance, ballast water or sediments from a ship is a reference to the discharge of the oil, oily mixture, noxious liquid substance, ballast water or sediments from the ship at any place in or outside Singapore; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a reference in this Act to the discharge of any oil, oily mixture, noxious liquid substance or sediments from a place on land is a reference to the discharge of the oil, oily mixture, noxious liquid substance or sediments from the place at any place in or outside Singapore.<div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any reference in this Act to the Convention, the Ballast Water Management Convention or any other international agreement shall be construed as including a reference to its protocols, annexes, appendices and other attachments.<div class="amendNote">[8/99]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 26 of 2017 wef 08/09/2017]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div
