<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Redemptorist Fathers Ordinance</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 374)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Ordinance 9 of 1948)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 1985</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(30th March 1987)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Ordinance to incorporate the Titular Superior of the Redemptorist Fathers in the Colony of Singapore.This private Ordinance is reproduced in the form it appears in the 1955 Revised Edition.<sup>&nbsp;</sup><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="FN"><sup>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</sup><em>Note: </em></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[23rd March 1948]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Ordinance may be cited as the Redemptorist Fathers Ordinance.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">The Titular Superior of the Redemptorist Fathers in the Colony of Singapore to be a body corporate</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong><a name="pr2-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Reverend Father WILLIAM DOWLING the Titular Superior of the Redemptorist Fathers in the Colony of Singapore, and his successors in office, shall be a body corporate (hereinafter called “the corporation”), and shall for the purposes of this Ordinance, have the name of “The Titular Superior of the Redemptorist Fathers in Singapore”, and by that name, have perpetual succession, and shall and may have and use a corporate seal.</span><a name="pr2-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The said seal may from time to time be broken, changed and altered, and made anew as to the corporation seems fit.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr2-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The expression “successors in office” shall be deemed to include the Reverend Father Minister from the time when the office of “The Titular Superior of the Redemptorist Fathers in Singapore” becomes vacant by the resignation or death of the holder for the time being, until the formal assumption of office by his successor.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to acquire and dispose of property</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong><a name="pr3-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The corporation may acquire, purchase, take, hold and enjoy movable and immovable property of every description, and may sell, convey, assign, exchange, surrender, yield up, mortgage, demise, reassign, transfer, or otherwise dispose of any movable or immovable property vested in the corporation upon such terms as to the corporation seems fit.</span><a name="pr3-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The corporation may sue and be sued in respect of such property in any of the Courts of the Colony of Singapore.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Use of the corporate seal</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;All deeds, documents and other instruments requiring the seal of the corporation shall be sealed with the seal of the corporation in the presence of the Titular Superior for the time being of the Redemptorist Fathers in Singapore, or when the office is vacant in the presence of the Reverend Father Minister, as the case may be, or the attorney of any one of them duly authorised by a Power of Attorney deposited under section&nbsp;48 of the Conveyancing and Law of Property Ordinance [1955 Ed., Cap. 243], and shall also be signed by the said Titular Superior for the time being of the Redemptorist Fathers in Singapore or by the said Reverend Father Minister, as the case may be, or the attorney of any one of them so authorised as aforesaid. </span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Such signing shall be and be taken as sufficient evidence that the said seal was duly and properly affixed, and that the same is the lawful seal of the corporation.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Notification of appointment of Titular Superior of the Redemptorist Fathers</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;A notification in the <em>Gazette</em> of the appointment of any person to exercise the office of Titular Superior of the Redemptorist Fathers in the Colony of Singapore, or of Reverend Father Minister, as the case may be, shall be conclusive evidence that such person was duly authorised to exercise the said office in the Colony.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Saving of  Government and other rights</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Ordinance shall affect the rights of the Government, all bodies politic and corporate, and all others, except such as are mentioned in this Ordinance and those claiming by, from or under them. <div class="amendNote">[7/97 wef 01/10/1997]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="fb27746e-167d-4fb1-85b9-ea053229a9a7"></div></div>
<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Saint Andrew’s Mission Hospital Ordinance</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 376)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Ordinance 42 of 1934)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 1985</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(30th March 1987)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Ordinance to incorporate Saint Andrew’s Mission Hospital. This private Ordinance is reproduced in the form it appears in the 1955 Revised Edition.<sup>&nbsp;</sup><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="FN"><sup>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</sup><em>Note:</em></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[28th December 1934]</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="preamble" id="ap-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">Whereas Mrs. Charlotte Elizabeth Ferguson-Davie, O.B.E., M.D., and her husband The Right Reverend Charles James Ferguson-Davie, then Bishop of Singapore, in or about the year 1913 in association with the Society for the Propagation of the Gospel inaugurated a Medical Mission under the style of St. Andrew’s Medical Mission, which established and maintained in Singapore with the aid of voluntary donations and subscriptions and grants from the Society for the Propagation of the Gospel dispensaries and a temporary hospital for indigent women and children without distinction of race, language or creed:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas on the application of the St. Andrew’s Medical Mission the Government agreed to provide land for the erection of a permanent hospital and dispensary and by an Indenture dated the 2nd day of&nbsp;March, 1922 made between His Excellency the Governor of the Colony for and on behalf of His Majesty the King of the one part and the Bishop of Singapore Incorporated, Teo Choon Hian, Ernest Charteris Holford Wolff, and Richard Myrrdin Williams (hereinafter called “the Trustees”) of the other part a certain piece of land situate at Erskine Road, Singapore containing in area 675 square metres and marked Lot 132<sup>5</sup> T.S. III in the Government Resurvey Map was demised to the Trustees for the term of 999 years upon trust to permit the same to be used for the erection of a Mission Hospital and Dispensary and to include such buildings and rooms as may be necessary or expedient in the opinion of the Committee of Management of the said Hospital and approved by Government and to be appropriated by the Committee as a Medical Mission Hospital and Dispensary for Women and Children without distinction of race, language or creed and to be known as the St. Andrew’s Medical Mission Hospital and to be managed in connection with the St. Andrew’s Medical Mission at Singapore and the Society for the Propagation of the Gospel:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas with the approval of the Government a building suitable for the requirements of a Hospital and Dispensary has been erected on the said piece of land with moneys raised by voluntary donations or subscriptions:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas the building was completed and the Hospital was opened in the year 1923 and the Hospital has since under the name of Saint Andrew’s Mission Hospital been maintained and carried on as a Christian Mission Hospital for poor women and children without distinction of race, language or creed by means of voluntary donations, subscriptions and grants-in-aid from the Society for the Propagation of the Gospel, The Singapore Diocesan Association, The Government, and the Municipal Commissioners of the Town of Singapore:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas since the year 1923 the Hospital has been managed by a Committee of Management constituted in the year 1923 in accordance with the recommendations of Mr. E. C. H. Wolff, M.C.S., and with the approval of Saint Andrew’s Medical Mission consisting of the Bishop of Singapore <em>ex-officio</em> Chairman, two members nominated by the Society for the Propagation of the Gospel, two members nominated by the Singapore Diocesan Association, one member representing the Presbyterian Church and another representing the Wesleyan Church (now known as the Methodist Episcopal Church) with the Secretary of St. Andrew’s Medical Mission as Honorary Secretary and an Honorary Treasurer Stanley James Vincent and eleven co-opted members, two from the Trustees, two from the larger donors to the fund, three from substantial subscribers, two from Medical Practitioners, two from the general public:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas the Committee of Management now called the Board of Management consider it expedient that the Parochial Church Council of Saint Andrew’s Cathedral should have the right to nominate two members of the Board of Management to be constituted by this Ordinance and two persons named in section&nbsp;20 of this Ordinance have accordingly been nominated by the Parochial Church Council of Saint Andrew’s Cathedral:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas the said Treasurer has inscribed in a book kept by him (hereinafter called “the Register of Subscribers”) the name of every person (firm and corporation) who has made a donation of not less than $500 to the building fund of the Hospital:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas it is expedient that the constitution and objects of the said Saint Andrew’s Mission Hospital be defined and declared by law and that provision be made by law for the management of the affairs and for the control of the property and funds thereof:</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="preambleText">And Whereas the Committee of Management have received the sums of money specified in Schedule <em>A</em> hereto upon trust to apply the same for the purposes therein described which sums of money are now invested in the manner described in Schedule <em>A</em>.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="enactWd" id="aw-">It is hereby enacted by the Governor of the Straits Settlements with the advice and consent of the Legislative Council thereof as follows:</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Ordinance may be cited as the Saint Andrew’s Mission Hospital Ordinance.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation and rights on incorporation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The persons constituting the present Committee of Management of St. Andrew’s Mission Hospital and the persons who for the time being are members of the Board of Management, hereinafter constituted and the persons and firms whose names are with their consent inscribed in the Register of Members mentioned in section&nbsp;8 hereof shall forever hereafter be one body corporate and politic by the name of Saint Andrew’s Mission Hospital (hereinafter called “the Corporation”) and by the same name shall have perpetual succession and a common seal with power to break, alter and make anew the said seal from time to time at their will and pleasure and by the same name shall and may sue and be sued in all Courts and in all manner of actions and suits and shall have power to do all other matters and things incidental or appertaining to a body corporate.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Powers</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Corporation may acquire, purchase, lease, take, hold and enjoy movable and immovable property of every description and, subject as hereinafter provided, may sell, convey, assign, surrender and yield up, mortgage, demise, reassign, transfer or otherwise dispose of any movable or immovable property vested in the Corporation upon such terms as to the Corporation may seem fit.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Vesting of property</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The said piece of land (being Lot 132<sup>5</sup> T.S. III) demised to the Trustees by the said Indenture together with the buildings erected thereon (which land and buildings are hereinafter called “the Hospital”) are hereby vested in the Corporation for the residue of the term of 999 years now subsisting therein for the purposes of this Ordinance freed from the trusts declared in the said Indenture but subject to the terms and conditions therein contained and all chattels, moneys, bonds, securities and property belonging to Saint Andrew’s Mission Hospital or any trustees on its behalf are hereby vested in the Corporation but as to the Bonds or securities specified in Schedule <em>A</em> hereto upon and for the trusts and purpose more particularly specified in Schedule <em>A</em> hereto.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sGrpTail" id="P4_5-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" style="text-transform:uppercase;">OBJECTS</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Objects and purposes</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong><a name="pr5-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The objects and general purposes for which the Corporation is established and incorporated are&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to take over the property vested in the Corporation by section&nbsp;4 hereof and to carry on and maintain the Hospital with all necessary furniture and other equipment as a Christian Mission Hospital and Dispensary for the treatment as in-patients or out-patients of women and children suffering from disease or accident without distinction of race, language or creed;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to instruct women in the proper care of their children;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to train Asiatic girls to nurse women and children;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to offer to those who desire it a knowledge of Christianity.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr5-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;To employ medical, surgical and pharmaceutical officers, nurses and attendants for the purposes aforesaid, and to provide and supply all such medical, surgical, and pharmaceutical appliances and things, and all such provisions and necessaries as may be required for the purposes aforesaid or any of them.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;To solicit and accept and receive subscriptions, donations, devises and bequests (whether of immovable or movable property and whether absolute or conditional) for the general purposes of the Corporation or for any special purpose of the Corporation or subject to any trust.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;To purchase or otherwise acquire land for any estate or interest and to erect buildings and maintain, alter and improve the same (including the Hospital) and to provide the same with light, water, drainage and other necessities.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;To raise money for any of the above purposes or other purposes of the Corporation by mortgaging or charging all or any of the property of the Corporation (other than the Hospital) with capital sums or with terminable annuities for lives or years.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;To hold, control and administer the moneys, funds, securities and property movable and immovable hereby vested in the Corporation or hereafter given to or in any manner acquired by or being in the custody or control of the Corporation and the income thereof, in accordance with the trusts or for the purposes affecting the same respectively, or in the absence of any special trust or purpose, for the general purposes of the Corporation and in particular to invest any money for the time being requiring investment in any investment authorised by law for trust funds or in the purchase of immovable property.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&nbsp;&nbsp;To do all such other lawful things as are incidental or conducive to the attainment of the above objects.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Application of income</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The income of the Corporation shall be applied solely towards the promotion of the objects of the Corporation as set forth in this Ordinance, and no portion thereof shall be paid or transferred directly or indirectly by way of dividend bonus or otherwise howsoever by way of profits to the members of the Corporation:<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="proviso" id="pr6-vi-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="provisoText" style="font-size:13pt">Provided that nothing herein contained shall prevent the payment in good faith of remuneration to any officers or servants of the Corporation or to any member thereof in return for services actually rendered to the Corporation or the payment of interest upon money borrowed from any member of the Corporation, or the payment to the donor of any money or securities or his or her nominee or nominees of any annuity by way of annual interest guaranteed by the Corporation on the amount of such gift during a period not exceeding the life of the donor or such nominee or nominees.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId"  <table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="PADate">The following Act was passed by Parliament on 17th August 2015 and assented to by the President on 21st August 2015:—</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="titlepg">Silver Support Scheme Act 2015</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="actNo">(No. 28 of 2015)</p><hr style="width:15%"><p class="sigTxtC">I assent.</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sigTbl" id="as-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="sig" id="as-sg-">TONY TAN KENG YAM,</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="position" id="as-sp-">President.</div><div class="sigDate"> 21st August 2015.</div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="cDateL">Date of Commencement: 18th January 2016 Part 1, section&nbsp;5, Parts 3 and 4</div><div class="cDateL">Date of Commencement: 22nd July 2016 Sections&nbsp;6 and 7</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act to provide for a social security scheme called the Silver Support Scheme and for related matters.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="enactWd" id="aw-">Be it enacted by the President with the advice and consent of the Parliament of Singapore, as follows:</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="part" id="P11-"><div class="partNo">PART 1</div><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P11-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title and commencement</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Silver Support Scheme Act 2015 and comes into operation on such date as the Minister may, by notification in the <em>Gazette</em>, appoint.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“administrator” means the Board, or any public officer or public authority appointed under section&nbsp;5(4) to assist the Board in administering the Scheme;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Board” means the Central Provident Fund Board constituted under section&nbsp;3 of the Central Provident Fund Act (Cap.&nbsp;36);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“cash grant” means any cash grant made by the Government under the Scheme;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Commissioner” means the Commissioner for Silver Support appointed under section&nbsp;4(1), and includes any Deputy Commissioner for Silver Support or Assistant Commissioner for Silver Support appointed under section&nbsp;4(2);</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“eligible individual” means an individual who is eligible to receive any benefit under the Scheme;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“investigator” means an officer or employee of the Board who is authorised under section&nbsp;5(7) to conduct any investigation under this Act, and includes any person appointed under section&nbsp;5(8) to assist the Board in conducting any investigation under this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“means information” means any information relating to the income or assets of any individual, or of a group of individuals who comprise a household, in the possession of any Government department or public authority;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“public authority” means a body established or constituted by or under a public Act to perform or discharge a public function;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“public scheme” means any scheme that&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">is or will be established by or under any written law and administered by a public authority, or by the Government in any other manner; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">is to provide financial relief, assistance or support to citizens or permanent residents of Singapore, or any part of them;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Scheme” means the Silver Support Scheme established under section&nbsp;5(1).</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Purpose of Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The purpose of this Act is to ensure that citizens of Singapore who are elderly, and who satisfy certain eligibility criteria, will receive financial support through a social security scheme.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Administration of Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong><a name="pr4-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may in writing appoint a public officer to be the Commissioner for Silver Support.</span><a name="pr4-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may in writing&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">appoint any public officer, or any employee of a public authority, to be a Deputy Commissioner for Silver Support; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">appoint any public officer, or any employee of a public authority, to be an Assistant Commissioner for Silver Support.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commissioner for Silver Support is responsible for the administration of this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr4-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the directions of the Commissioner for Silver Support, every Deputy Commissioner for Silver Support and every Assistant Commissioner for Silver Support may perform the functions and exercise the powers of the Commissioner for Silver Support.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="ajax-loading">&nbsp;</div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="09dc5229-e642-4e8e-8ab5-3ab53812dcfc"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="7b37c886-e2a4-4d7e-8183-193354b89788"></div><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="2f0b114d-75d0-4016-ac52-59bb800e63d0"></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="d0e3de28-fb97-4920-8c79-b51fc326a021"></div></div>
<div class="front"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="actHd" id="aT-">Singapore Tourism (Cess Collection) Act</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="chapNo">(CHAPTER 305C)</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="origSrc">(Original Enactment: Act 1 of 1972)</p><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdHdr">REVISED EDITION 1997</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="revdTxt">(20th December 1997)</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="longTitle" id="al-">An Act for the collection of cess by the Singapore Tourism Board.</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="cDate">[6th February 1973]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="body"><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act may be cited as the Singapore Tourism (Cess Collection) Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&nbsp;—<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Board” means the Singapore Tourism Board established under section&nbsp;3 of the Singapore Tourism Board Act (Cap. 305B) and includes any agent duly appointed by the Board to act on its behalf;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Chief Executive” means the Chief Executive of the Board and includes any acting Chief Executive of the Board;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“Fund” means the Tourism Fund established under section&nbsp;15 of the Singapore Tourism Board Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><span id="pr2-pd-oc1-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="definitionRepealed">[<em>Deleted by Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“product” means any one or more of the following: <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any travel product within the meaning of the Travel Agents Act (Cap.&nbsp;334);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any goods (including any food or beverage intended for human consumption);<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><span id="pr2-pd-oc2-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="definitionRepealed">[<em>Deleted by Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“record” means any record of information however recorded, and includes&nbsp;— <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">anything on which there is writing or Braille; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">a map, plan, chart, graph, picture or photograph;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">anything from which images, sounds or writing can be reproduced; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">anything on which information has been stored or recorded; <div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“service” means any service relating to any one or more of the following: <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">arts or entertainment;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">leisure, recreation or sports;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">personal care, wellness or assistance;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">transport, other than transport by use of a regular route service within the meaning of the Bus Services Industry Act&nbsp;2015 (Act&nbsp;30 of 2015) or a train service within the meaning of the Public Transport Council Act (Cap.&nbsp;259B);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">business meetings, incentive travel, conferences, conventions and exhibitions (commonly known as MICE);<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“taxable transaction connected with a tourism event” has the meaning given by section&nbsp;5(2);<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“tourism event” means any event or series of related activities taking place in Singapore&nbsp;— <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">that promotes Singapore as a travel or tourist destination; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">that is intended wholly or partly for the benefit of, or for the purpose of attracting, visitors to Singapore; <div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“tourism event establishment” means a person prescribed in an order made under section&nbsp;5; <div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“tourism event premises” means any premises used or to be used for the conduct of a tourism event by the organiser of that event;<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><span id="pr2-pd-oc3-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="definitionRepealed">[<em>Deleted by Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table><span id="pr2-pd-oc4-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="definitionRepealed">[<em>Deleted by Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table><span id="pr2-pd-oc5-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="definitionRepealed">[<em>Deleted by Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“transaction” means any arrangement made by a person in the course of carrying on a business in Singapore&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for the provision, or to facilitate the provision, of the use of any tourism event premises, accommodation, products or services, to another person; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">where the use of any tourism event premises, accommodation, products or services in contemplation of which an arrangement in paragraph&nbsp;(<em>a</em>) was made does not take place, </td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="defSO" style="font-size:13pt">whether or not&nbsp;—</td></tr></tbody></table><table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(i)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the other person is in Singapore;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(ii)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the arrangement is at the request of the other person; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(iii)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any consideration is given for the arrangement.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></span></span></span></span></span></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Application of Act</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2A.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;This Act does not apply to any tourism event premises, accommodation, product or service provided or to be provided by the Government, or a body established by or under a public Act for a public purpose.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Delegation of functions</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong><a name="pr3-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board may appoint such agents (including the Government) as may be necessary for the purposes of this Act.</span><a name="pr3-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board may delegate all or any of the powers and functions under this Act relating to or appertaining to the collection of cess to any person including an officer or department of the Government.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr3-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board may pay to any person appointed under subsection&nbsp;(1) a fee for the services rendered in connection with the collection of cess.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr4-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Cess to be paid into Fund</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>4.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;All moneys collected under this Act shall be paid into the Fund.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr5-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Cess payable</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>5.</strong><a name="pr5-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Cess is payable at the amount prescribed by the Minister by order in the <em>Gazette</em> on every taxable transaction connected (in the manner provided in subsection&nbsp;(2)) with a tourism event to which the order relates.</span><a name="pr5-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this Act, a transaction is a taxable transaction connected with a tourism event if&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the use of the tourism event premises, accommodation, product or service under the transaction is or is to be provided, or (where paragraph&nbsp;(<em>b</em>) of the definition of “transaction” in section&nbsp;2 applies) could have been provided, during a period during which the tourism event is held, being a period which may include any time before or after the event is held (called in this section a taxable period); and </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the transaction, which satisfies paragraph&nbsp;(<em>a</em>), is prescribed in an order under subsection&nbsp;(1) to be a taxable transaction connected with that tourism event.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;A transaction is not to be treated as other than a taxable transaction by reason only that&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the transaction is made with a person who is not a visitor to Singapore; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the transaction is made for any purpose other than for purposes of any tourism event;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the transaction is terminated for any reason; or </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the tourism event premises, accommodation, product or service to be provided under the transaction, is not provided or used for any reason.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;An order under subsection&nbsp;(1) must specify or describe&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the tourism event to which the order relates;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the taxable transactions connected with a tourism event on which cess is payable;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the tourism event establishments making the taxable transactions connected with a tourism event;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the taxable period for the taxable transactions connected with a tourism event; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the amount of the cess.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purposes of subsection&nbsp;(4)(<em>e</em>), the amount of cess payable on a taxable transaction connected with a tourism event may be prescribed in an order under subsection&nbsp;(1) as a rate based on&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the gross receipts derived from the taxable transaction; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">an amount treated as the gross receipts derived from the taxable transaction&nbsp;—<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr5-ps5-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">that is terminated; or</td></tr><tr id="pr5-ps5-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">for which no or partial consideration is given,</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">and the order may further provide for the method by which such gross receipts or amount treated as the gross receipts are to be determined.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;An order under subsection&nbsp;(1) may prescribe different taxable periods, different amounts of cess, or different methods of determining the gross receipts or amounts treated as the gross receipts&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for different taxable transactions connected with a tourism event;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for different tourism event premises, accommodation, products or services; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for different tourism events or tourism event establishments; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">on any other differential basis.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&nbsp;&nbsp;In determining the “gross receipts” or “an amount treated as the gross receipts”, there must be excluded the amount of any goods and services tax chargeable on any supply of goods or services comprised in that taxable transaction connected with a tourism event.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr5-ps8-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(8)&nbsp;&nbsp;No person is relieved from liability to pay cess on a taxable transaction connected with a tourism event by reason of the fact that the person ceases during a taxable period to carry on business in Singapore.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr6-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Tourism event establishment liable to pay cess</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>6.</strong><a name="pr6-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Cess payable on a taxable transaction connected with a tourism event is payable by the tourism event establishment making the taxable transaction.</span><a name="pr6-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Cess must be accounted for and paid within the time prescribed by regulations made under this Act. </td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr6-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Cess must be paid to the Board in the manner required by the Board.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1Rep" id="pr7-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1RepText"><strong>7.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;[<em>Repealed by Act 16/2008 wef 19/09/2008</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr8-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to enter premises, etc.</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>8.</strong><a name="pr8-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chief Executive, or an officer or agent of the Board authorised by the Chief Executive, is entitled, at all reasonable times, to full and free access to any premises that the Chief Executive, officer or agent (as the case may be) reasonably believes are relevant premises, to do all or any of the following for relevant purposes:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to inspect the premises; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">without any fee or reward, to inspect, make copies of, or take extracts from, any record; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">to take possession of any record if, in the opinion of the Chief Executive, officer or agent, as the case may be&nbsp;— <table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr8-ps1-p1c-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">the inspection or copy of, or extract from, the record cannot reasonably be performed without taking possession;</td></tr><tr id="pr8-ps1-p1c-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the record may be interfered with or destroyed unless possession is taken; or</td></tr><tr id="pr8-ps1-p1c-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the record may be required as evidence in proceedings for an offence under this Act or any regulations made under this Act, or in proceedings for the recovery of cess.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr8-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section&nbsp;— <table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“relevant premises” means&nbsp;— <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any premises owned or occupied by a person who is, or could be prescribed as, a tourism event establishment; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any premises where any record relating to cess payable under this Act is or is likely to be kept; </td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“relevant purposes” means any one or both of the following purposes: <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to administer or enforce this Act or any order or regulations made under this Act, including to enable the Board to ascertain the amount of cess payable by any person under this Act;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">to enable the Board to provide its views to the Minister on any matter to be prescribed in an order to be made under section&nbsp;5.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr9-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Keeping of records and giving of receipts</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>9.</strong><a name="pr9-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to subsection&nbsp;(2), every person liable to pay cess under the provisions of this Act shall keep and retain for a minimum period  in safe custody&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">records provided by the person under section&nbsp;8(1) to the Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board authorised by the Chief Executive;<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>aa</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">records of the information provided by the person under section&nbsp;10(3) to the Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board authorised by the Chief Executive; and<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">sufficient records to enable the amount of cess payable under any order made under section&nbsp;5 to be readily ascertained by the Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board authorised by the Chief Executive.<div class="amendNote">[16/2008 wef 19/09/2008]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr9-ps1A-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(1A)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a machine is used for recording taxable transactions connected with a tourism event, receipts of those transactions may be dispensed with if the Chief Executive, or an officer or agent of the Board authorised by the Chief Executive, is satisfied that&nbsp;— <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the machine records all of those transactions; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a record of all of those transactions for each day and (if applicable) the consideration given for each transaction, is made by the end of each day; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the record mentioned in paragraph&nbsp;(<em>b</em>) fulfils the requirements of subsection&nbsp;(1)(<em>b</em>).<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board duly authorised by the Chief Executive in that behalf may in respect of any class or description of persons who are liable to pay cess under this Act&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">direct them to keep and retain the records referred to in subsection&nbsp;(1)(<em>a</em>) and (<em>aa</em>) in the form and manner approved by the Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board, as the case may be;<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">direct them to issue and retain the receipts and their duplicates referred to in subsection&nbsp;(1)(<em>b</em>) in the form and manner approved by the Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board, as the case may be.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board duly authorised by the Chief Executive in that behalf may waive all or any of the provisions of subsection&nbsp;(1) or (1A) in respect of any person or records or any class of persons or records.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section, “minimum period”, in relation to the keeping and retention of a record, means&nbsp;— <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">subject to paragraph&nbsp;(<em>b</em>), for every record provided or made before the date of commencement of section&nbsp;6 of the Singapore Tourism (Cess Collection) (Amendment) Act&nbsp;2018&nbsp;— 2 years after the record was provided or made, as the case may be; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for every record provided (whenever made) or made on or after the date of commencement of section&nbsp;6 of the Singapore Tourism (Cess Collection) (Amendment) Act 2018&nbsp;— 5 years (or such longer period as may be prescribed in substitution by regulations made under this Act) after the record was provided or made, as the case may be.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr9-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who contravenes or fails to comply with this section or any direction of the Chief Executive or an officer or agent of the Board issued pursuant to this section shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $5,000.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr10-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Duty to inform</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>10.</strong><a name="pr10-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every person liable to pay cess under this Act shall, within 7 days of the date of commencement or cessation of any business carried on by him in respect of which cess is payable on any transaction relating thereto, inform the Board in writing of the business carried on by him.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></span><a name="pr10-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Every person liable to pay cess under this Act shall inform the Board in writing of any change of his place of business.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr10-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chief Executive, or an officer or agent of the Board authorised by the Chief Executive, may, by written notice under subsection&nbsp;(3A), require any person to provide the Chief Executive, officer or agent with information that the Chief Executive, officer or agent (as the case may be) considers necessary for any one or both of the relevant purposes mentioned in section&nbsp;8(2).<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr10-ps3A-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3A)&nbsp;&nbsp;The written notice may specify&nbsp;— <table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the form and manner in which the information must be provided; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the time by which the information must be provided; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the frequency with which the information must be provided during a period specified in the written notice, which period must not exceed 5&nbsp;years (or such longer period as may be prescribed in substitution by regulations made under this Act) after the date of the written notice.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr10-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who contravenes or fails to comply with subsection&nbsp;(1), (2) or (3) shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $5,000.<div class="amendNote">[16/2008 wef 19/09/2008]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Recovery of cess</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to any other remedy, any cess payable under this Act may be recovered as a debt due to the Board from the person accountable therefor.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Recovery of cess on basis of Board’s estimate</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12.</strong><a name="pr12-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an amount is due from any person on account of cess, and such cess is not accounted for and paid to the Board within the prescribed time, the Board may estimate the amount of cess due.</span><a name="pr12-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an amount is due from any person on account of cess, but by reason of his failure to keep or to produce or furnish to the Board the accounts or records required by this Act or any regulations made thereunder or to take or permit to be taken any other step which he is so required to take or permit to be taken or by reason of the accounts or records kept, produced or furnished being materially incomplete or inaccurate, the Board is unable to ascertain the amount of cess properly due from him, the Board may estimate the amount of cess due.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an estimate of the amount of cess due from any person has been made under subsection&nbsp;(1) or (2), then (without prejudice to the recovery of the full amount due or to the making of a further estimate in that behalf) the amount estimated shall be recoverable as cess properly due unless in an action relating thereto the person liable proves the amount properly due and that amount is less than the amount estimated.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an estimate of the amount of cess due from any person has been made under subsection&nbsp;(1) or (2), that person shall pay the amount estimated together with the penalty (if any) imposed by section&nbsp;13 within 7 days of the receipt of the notice from the Board requiring him to pay the cess.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr13-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Penalty</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>13.</strong><a name="pr13-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to subsection&nbsp;(1A), if any cess is not accounted for and paid within the time prescribed by the Board&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a penalty equal to 5% of the amount of cess payable whether estimated or not shall be added thereto; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">if the amount of cess outstanding is not paid within 60&nbsp;days of the imposition of the penalty as provided by paragraph&nbsp;(<em>a</em>), an additional penalty of 2% of the cess outstanding shall be payable for each completed month that the cess remains unpaid commencing from the date on which the cess became payable, except that the total additional penalty shall not exceed 50% of the amount of cess outstanding.<div class="amendNote">[16/2008 wef 19/09/2008]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr13-ps1A-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(1A)&nbsp;&nbsp;The provisions of this Act relating to the collection and recovery of cess shall apply to the collection and recovery of the penalty and additional penalty.<div class="amendNote">[16/2008 wef 19/09/2008]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr13-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board may, for any good cause shown, reduce or remit the whole or part of the penalty due under subsection&nbsp;(1).</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr14-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Suit for cess and penalty by Board</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>14.</strong><a name="pr14-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding the provisions of any other written law, cess and any penalty imposed under this Act may be sued for by way of a specially endorsed writ of summons and the Board shall be entitled to all costs allowed by law against the person liable thereto.</span><a name="pr14-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In any suit under subsection&nbsp;(1), the production of a certificate signed by the Chief Executive giving the name and address of the defendant and the amount of cess and penalty due by him shall be sufficient evidence of the amount so due and sufficient authority for the court to give judgment for that amount.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr15-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Refund or return of cess or penalty overpaid or erroneously paid</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>15.</strong><a name="pr15-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as provided in this section, no person is entitled to any refund of any money that was overpaid, or return of any money that was erroneously paid, as cess or penalty under this Act.</span><a name="pr15-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person who overpaid or erroneously paid any money as cess or penalty under this Act may make a claim to the Board for the refund of the money overpaid or return of the money erroneously paid.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr15-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;A refund or return to a person of any money that is the subject of a claim under subsection&nbsp;(2) may be made only if&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person makes the claim within one year after the date of the overpayment or erroneous payment; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the claim is in the form and manner required by the Board; and </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Board is satisfied that there was an overpayment or erroneous payment.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr16-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Payment of underpaid cess or penalty, etc.</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>16.</strong><a name="pr16-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;This section applies where for any reason or owing to any cause, a person underpays any cess or penalty under this Act, or is refunded or returned any money under section&nbsp;15 despite not being entitled to such refund or return.</span><a name="pr16-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The person mentioned in subsection&nbsp;(1) must, on demand being made by the Board within one year after the date of the underpayment, or erroneous refund or return, pay the deficiency or repay the money erroneously refunded or returned (as the case may be) to the Board.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr17-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Incorrect return</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>17.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who makes an incorrect return under this Act or any regulations made thereunder by omitting therefrom any information or gives any incorrect information to the Chief Executive or the Board under section&nbsp;10 shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $5,000 and in default of payment to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months.<div class="amendNote">[16/2008 wef 19/09/2008]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr18-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Evasion of cess</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>18.</strong><a name="pr18-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who wilfully with intent to evade or to assist any other person to evade cess&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">omits from a return made under this Act or any regulations made thereunder any information in relation to any matter affecting the amount of cess payable which should be included;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">makes a false statement or entry in any return made under this Act or any regulations made thereunder;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">gives any false answer whether verbally or in writing to any question or request for information asked or made in accordance with the provisions of this Act or any regulations made thereunder;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">prepares or maintains or authorises the preparation or maintenance of any false book of accounts or other records or falsifies or authorises the falsification of any book of accounts or other records; or<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">makes use of any fraud, art or contrivance whatsoever or authorises the use of any such fraud, art or contrivance,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $5,000 or to imprisonment for a term of not less than 6 months or to both.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr18-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Whenever in any proceedings under this section it is proved that any false statement or entry is made in any return furnished under this Act or any regulations made thereunder by or on behalf of any person or any book of accounts or other records maintained by or on behalf of any person, that person shall be presumed, until the contrary is proved, to have made that false statement or entry with intent to evade cess.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr19-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Obstructing officer of Board</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>19.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who obstructs or hinders any officer or agent of the Board acting in the discharge of his duty under this Act or any regulations made thereunder shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $5,000.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr20-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to exempt and remit</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>20.</strong><a name="pr20-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order in the <em>Gazette</em>, exempt any person or class of persons from all or any of the provisions of this Act, either generally or in a particular case and subject to such conditions as the Minister may impose.</span><a name="pr20-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may remit the whole or any part of the cess payable by any person under this Act, if the Minister is satisfied that it is just and equitable to do so.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr20-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board must, following the Minister’s decision under subsection&nbsp;(2) and if the amount remitted has been paid to the Board by the person mentioned in that subsection, return that amount to the person.<div class="amendNote">[Act 28 of 2018 wef 06/09/2018]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1Rep" id="pr21-"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1RepText"><strong>21.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;[<em>Repealed by Act 16/2008 wef 19/09/2008</em>]</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr22-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Proceedings conducted by officer of Board</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>22.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Proceedings in respect of any offence under this Act or any regulations made thereunder may, with the authorisation of the Public Prosecutor, be conducted by an officer of the Board or an officer of the Government authorised in writing in that behalf by the Chief Executive.<div class="amendNote">[15/2010 wef 02/01/2011]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr23-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Consent of Public Prosecutor</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>23.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;No court shall try any offence under this Act or any regulations made thereunder except with the consent of the Public Prosecutor.<div class="amendNote">[15/2010 wef 02/01/2011]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr24-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Priority of case in bankruptcy</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>24.</strong><a name="pr24-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall be included among the debts which, under section 352 of the Insolvency, Restructuring and Dissolution Act 2018, are to be paid in priority to all other debts in the distribution of property of a bankrupt or a person dying insolvent, the amount of any cess due from the bankrupt at the date of the bankruptcy order, or from the person so dying at the date of his death, and having become due within 12 months before that date.<div class="amendNote">[Act 40 of 2018 wef 30/07/2020]</div></span><a name="pr24-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall be included among the taxes which, under section&nbsp;203 of the Insolvency, Restructuring and Dissolution Act 2018, are to be paid in priority to all other unsecured debts in a winding up of a company, the amount of any cess due from the company and having become due within 12 months before the date of commencement of the winding up.<div class="amendNote">[Act 40 of 2018 wef 30/07/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr25-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Offence by body corporate</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>25.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an offence under this Act or any regulations made thereunder has been committed by a body corporate and is found to have been committed with the consent of, connivance of or to be attributable to any act or default on the part of any director, manager, secretary or other officer, the director, manager, secretary or other officer as well as the body corporate shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $5,000.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr26-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Regulations</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>26.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board may, with the approval of the Minister, make such regulations as are necessary for carrying into effect the provisions of this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr27-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Transitional provision</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>27.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any subsidiary legislation made under the Singapore Tourism Board Act (Cap. 305B) relating to the matters falling within the scope of this Act which is not inconsistent with the provisions of this Act shall remain in force and shall be deemed to be made under this Act until it has been revoked or replaced by subsidiary legislation made under this Act.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="tail"><div class="schedule"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td
