which accompanies a seized wildlife;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any other thing which appears to be or to contain evidence of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr11B-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to subsection (4), when any wildlife, article, conveyance or other thing is seized under subsection (1), the enforcement officer who seized it must —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">arrange for the seized item to be removed to and detained in a compound, enclosure or other place determined by the Director-General or an authorised officer for that purpose; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">report the seizure and detention to a Magistrate.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr11B-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Magistrate may order the further detention or the release of the seized item.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr11B-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the seized item is perishable, the Director-General or an authorised officer may dispose of it in any manner the Director-General or authorised officer thinks fit.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr11B-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Director-General or an authorised officer may subject the seized item to any examination or analysis that the Director-General or authorised officer (as the case may be) considers necessary for the purposes of this Act.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11C-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Enforcement officer’s assistants</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11C.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;An enforcement officer may be accompanied or assisted by persons necessary for the exercise of the enforcement officer’s powers under section 10A, 11A or 11B.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Power to arrest without warrant</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12.</strong><a name="pr12-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any police officer, officer of customs or authorised officer may stop and arrest without warrant any person who within his view commits an offence under this Act.<div class="amendNote">[16/2000]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></span><a name="pr12-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Such person shall not be arrested if he satisfies the police officer, officer of customs or authorised officer as to his name and residence in Singapore and that he does not intend to abscond.<div class="pREProvNo">[11</div><div class="amendNote">[16/2000]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;Any person who, without reasonable excuse&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">refuses or fails to comply with a request of a police officer, an officer of customs or an authorised officer under this section for the person’s name and residence in Singapore; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in response to the request, gives a name that is false in a material particular, or gives an address other than the person’s full and correct residential address,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $10,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months or to both.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="amendNote">[Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;A police officer, an officer of customs or an authorised officer making an arrest under subsection&nbsp;(1) must not restrain the person arrested more than is necessary to prevent the person’s escape.<div class="amendNote">[Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person arrested under this section may be detained until his name and address are correctly ascertained except that a person so arrested must not be detained longer than is permitted by written law and is necessary for bringing him before a court unless the order of a court for his detention is obtained.<div class="amendNote">[Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Powers of examination</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12A.</strong><a name="pr12A-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;For the purpose of investigating any offence under this Act, the Director-General or an authorised officer may&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">examine orally any person supposed to be acquainted with the facts and circumstances of the case; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by written order require any person within the limits of Singapore, who appears to be acquainted with the facts and circumstances of the case, to attend before the Director-General or authorised officer.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12A-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The person mentioned in subsection&nbsp;(1)(<em>a</em>) is bound to state truly the facts and circumstances with which the person is acquainted concerning the case except only that the person may decline to make, with regard to any fact or circumstance, a statement which would have a tendency to expose the person to a criminal charge or to penalty or forfeiture.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12A-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;A statement made by any person examined under this section must&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">be reduced to writing;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">be read over to the person;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">if the person does not understand English, be interpreted in a language that the person understands; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">after correction (if necessary), be signed by the person.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12A-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;If any person fails to attend before the Director-General or an authorised officer as required by an order under subsection&nbsp;(1)(<em>b</em>), the Director-General or authorised officer may report the failure to a Magistrate who may issue a warrant to secure the attendance of that person as required by the order.<div class="amendNote">[Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12B-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Powers to require information, etc., about contraventions</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12B.</strong><a name="pr12B-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where it appears to the Director-General or an authorised officer that there may have been a contravention of any provision of this Act, the Director-General or authorised officer may serve an information notice to require any person who appears to him to be acquainted with the circumstances of the case to furnish the Director-General or authorised officer (as the case may be), within such time as may be specified in the notice, with information relating to that case in the possession or within the knowledge of that person.</span><a name="pr12B-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;An information notice under subsection&nbsp;(1) must be complied with by giving the required information in writing to the Director-General or authorised officer, as the case may be.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12B-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Director-General or an authorised officer may serve a production notice to require any person who is reasonably believed to have any document or article in the person’s possession, custody or control relating to the contravention mentioned in subsection (1) to produce that document or article within the time specified in the notice.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12B-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person who is served an information notice under subsection (1) may decline to furnish the required information if it would have a tendency to expose the person to a criminal charge or to penalty or forfeiture.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12B-ps4A-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4A)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person who, without reasonable excuse, fails to comply with an information notice under subsection (1), or a production notice under subsection (3), shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $10,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months or to both.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12B-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;If any person&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">makes any statement purporting to comply with a requirement of an information notice which the person knows to be false or misleading in a material particular; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">recklessly makes such a statement which is false or misleading in a material particular,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">the person shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $10,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months or to both.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="amendNote">[Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12C-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Forfeiture by court in criminal proceedings</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12C.</strong><a name="pr12C-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;A court may, in proceedings where a person is tried for an offence under this Act, order that a seized item in connection with the offence be forfeited to the Director-General if —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the seized item is a conveyance — the person is convicted of the offence and the conveyance is proved to have been used in the commission of the offence; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the seized item is not a conveyance — the court is satisfied that the offence has been committed and that the seized item was the subject matter, or used (or intended to have been used) in the commission, or constitutes evidence, of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12C-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Subsection (1)(<em>a</em>) does not apply to a conveyance which —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is of more than 200 tons net; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is an aircraft or a train belonging to a person carrying on a regular passenger service to and from Singapore by means of that aircraft or train.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12C-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;The court may consider the question of forfeiture under subsection (1) on its own motion if no party raises the question in the proceedings before the court.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12C-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;A conveyance mentioned in subsection (1)(<em>a</em>) must not be forfeited under that provision if its owner establishes that the conveyance was unlawfully in the possession of another person without the consent of the owner.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12C-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;The court may make an order under subsection (1)(<em>b</em>) for the forfeiture of any seized item despite that no person is convicted of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12C-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;The court must order the release of a seized item to the owner of or the person entitled to the seized item if —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the court, having regard to the circumstances of the case, does not think it fit to order the forfeiture of the seized item under subsection (1);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the requirements of subsection (1)(<em>a</em>) or (<em>b</em>) (as the case may be) are not met; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the seized item is a conveyance mentioned in subsection (2) or (4).<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12D-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Forfeiture in other circumstances</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12D.</strong><a name="pr12D-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where section 12C does not apply, the Director-General must give the person from whom the item was seized and the owner (if known) of the item a written notice requiring any claim for the item to be made in accordance with subsection (2) within the time specified in the notice.</span><a name="pr12D-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person who wishes to claim a seized item mentioned in subsection (1) (called in this section the claimant) must submit, either personally or through an authorised agent, a written claim (containing the basis of the claimant’s claim) to the Director-General.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12D-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;On receiving the written claim under subsection (2), the Director-General may direct that the seized item be released to the claimant or refer the matter to a court for decision.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12D-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;If no claim is received for the seized item within the period stated in the notice mentioned in subsection (1) —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case where the seized item is a conveyance, the Director-General must refer the matter to a court for decision; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in any other case, the seized item is forfeited to the Director-General.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12D-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;If the owner of a seized item (other than a conveyance) mentioned in subsection (1) consents to its disposal by the Director-General, the seized item is forfeited to the Director-General.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12D-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section, “authorised agent”, for a claimant, means a person who is designated in writing by the claimant as the claimant’s authorised agent for the purposes of this section.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12E-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Director-General’s powers after forfeiture</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12E.</strong><a name="pr12E-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where any item is forfeited to the Director-General under section 12C or 12D, the Director-General may —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case where the item is a wildlife which was imported or introduced into Singapore in a conveyance in contravention of this Act, direct the owner of the conveyance to repatriate the wildlife to the place from which the wildlife was imported or introduced into Singapore or any other place designated by the Director-General; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">dispose of the item in any manner the Director-General thinks fit.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12E-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The owner of a conveyance who is directed to repatriate a wildlife under subsection (1)(<em>a</em>) must, at that owner’s own expense, arrange for —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the repatriation of the wildlife in accordance with the direction; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the proper care and maintenance of the wildlife during the repatriation.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12E-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person is not required to comply with subsection (2) in respect of a direction made under subsection (1)(<em>a</em>) unless the direction is made within —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">12 months after the date on which the wildlife mentioned in the direction was imported or introduced into Singapore; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">6 months after the date on which proceedings for the offence in connection with that importation or introduction are concluded or the date on which the offence is compounded,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">whichever is the later.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12E-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person who, without reasonable excuse, contravenes subsection (2) shall be guilty of an offence and shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $10,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months or to both.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12F-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Expenses</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12F.</strong><a name="pr12F-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The following persons are responsible for any expenses incurred by the Director-General or any enforcement officer for the seizure, detention, storage, housing, maintenance, transport, repatriation or disposal of any seized item:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case where the item is a wildlife which was imported or introduced into Singapore in contravention of this Act, the owner and the importer of the wildlife (jointly and severally);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case where the item is a wildlife which was being exported from Singapore in contravention of this Act, the owner and the exporter of the wildlife (jointly and severally);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in any other case, the owner of the item.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12F-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;If the amount of the expenses mentioned in subsection (1) is not paid by the person responsible for the expenses under that subsection within 14 days after demand, the amount may be reported to a Magistrate’s Court or a District Court and recovered in the same manner as if it were a fine imposed by a Magistrate’s Court or a District Court.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12G-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Obstruction</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12G.</strong><a name="pr12G-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person commits an offence if the person, without reasonable excuse, obstructs or hinders the Director-General or an enforcement officer in the exercise of any power or performance of any function under this Act.</span><a name="pr12G-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person who is guilty of an offence under subsection (1) shall be liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding $10,000 or to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months or to both.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12H-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Offences by employee or agent</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12H.</strong><a name="pr12H-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an offence under this Act is committed by an employee (in the course of employment) or an agent (in the course of acting as an agent) of a person (called in this section the defendant), the defendant shall be guilty of that same offence as is the employee or agent (as the case may be), and shall be liable on conviction to be punished accordingly if the defendant —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">consented or connived to effect the commission of the offence;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">is in any other way, whether by act or omission, knowingly concerned in, or party to, the commission of the offence by the employee or agent; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">knew or ought reasonably to have known that the offence by the employee or agent (or an offence of the same type) would be or is being committed, and failed to take all reasonable steps to prevent or stop the commission of that offence.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12H-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;The defendant may rely on a defence that would be available to the employee or agent if the employee or agent were charged with the offence with which the defendant is charged and, in doing so, the defendant bears the same burden of proof that the employee or agent would bear.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12H-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, this section does not affect —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the application of Chapters V and VA of the Penal Code, the Evidence Act (Cap. 97) or any other law or practice regarding the admissibility of evidence; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the liability of an employee or agent for an offence under this Act, and applies whether or not the employee or agent is convicted of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12H-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;A reference in this section to an employee or agent of a defendant does not include —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the defendant is a corporation, an individual mentioned in section 12I(2)(<em>a</em>) in relation to a corporation; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the defendant is an unincorporated association or a partnership, an individual mentioned in section 12J(2)(<em>a</em>) in relation to an unincorporated association or a partnership.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12I-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Offences by corporations</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12I.</strong><a name="pr12I-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where, in a proceeding for an offence under this Act, it is necessary to prove the state of mind of a corporation in relation to a particular conduct, evidence that —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">an officer, employee or agent of the corporation engaged in that conduct within the scope of his actual or apparent authority; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the officer, employee or agent had that state of mind,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">is evidence that the corporation had that state of mind.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12I-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a corporation commits an offence under this Act, a person —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">who is —<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr12I-ps2-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">an officer of the corporation; or</td></tr><tr id="pr12I-ps2-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">an individual involved in the management of the corporation and in a position to influence the conduct of the corporation in relation to the commission of the offence; and</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">who —<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr12I-ps2-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">consented or connived, or conspired with others, to effect the commission of the offence;</td></tr><tr id="pr12I-ps2-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">is in any other way, whether by act or omission, knowingly concerned in, or party to, the commission of the offence by the corporation; or</td></tr><tr id="pr12I-ps2-p1b-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">knew or ought reasonably to have known that the offence by the corporation (or an offence of the same type) would be or is being committed, and failed to take all reasonable steps to prevent or stop the commission of that offence,</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">shall be guilty of that same offence as is the corporation, and shall be liable on conviction to be punished accordingly.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12I-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person mentioned in subsection (2) may rely on a defence that would be available to the corporation if it were charged with the offence with which the person is charged and, in doing so, the person bears the same burden of proof that the corporation would bear.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12I-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, this section does not affect the application of&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">Chapters V and VA of the Penal Code; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Evidence Act or any other law or practice regarding the admissibility of evidence.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12I-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, subsection (2) does not affect the liability of the corporation for an offence under this Act, and applies whether or not the corporation is convicted of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12I-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section —<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“corporation” includes a limited liability partnership;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“officer”, in relation to a corporation, means any director, partner, chief executive, manager, secretary or other similar officer of the corporation, and includes —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any person purporting to act in any such capacity; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">for a corporation whose affairs are managed by its members, any of those members as if the member were a director of the corporation;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“state of mind” of a person includes —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the knowledge, intention, opinion, belief or purpose of the person; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the person’s reasons for the intention, opinion, belief or purpose.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12J-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Offences by unincorporated associations or partnerships</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12J.</strong><a name="pr12J-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where, in a proceeding for an offence under this Act, it is necessary to prove the state of mind of an unincorporated association or a partnership in relation to a particular conduct, evidence that —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">an employee or agent of the unincorporated association or partnership engaged in that conduct within the scope of his actual or apparent authority; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the employee or agent had that state of mind,</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">is evidence that the unincorporated association or partnership had that state of mind.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12J-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where an unincorporated association or a partnership commits an offence under this Act, a person —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">who is —<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr12J-ps2-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">an officer of the unincorporated association or a member of its governing body;</td></tr><tr id="pr12J-ps2-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">a partner in the partnership; or</td></tr><tr id="pr12J-ps2-p1a-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">an individual involved in the management of the unincorporated association or partnership and in a position to influence the conduct of the unincorporated association or partnership (as the case may be) in relation to the commission of the offence; and</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">who —<table class="p2_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr id="pr12J-ps2-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">consented or connived, or conspired with others, to effect the commission of the offence;</td></tr><tr id="pr12J-ps2-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">is in any other way, whether by act or omission, knowingly concerned in, or party to, the commission of the offence by the unincorporated association or partnership; or</td></tr><tr id="pr12J-ps2-p1b-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">knew or ought reasonably to have known that the offence by the unincorporated association or partnership (or an offence of the same type) would be or is being committed, and failed to take all reasonable steps to prevent or stop the commission of that offence,</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1N2SO" style="font-size:13pt">shall be guilty of that same offence as is the unincorporated association or partnership (as the case may be), and shall be liable on conviction to be punished accordingly.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12J-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;A person mentioned in subsection (2) may rely on a defence that would be available to the unincorporated association or partnership if it were charged with the offence with which the person is charged and, in doing so, the person bears the same burden of proof as the unincorporated association or partnership would bear.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12J-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, this section does not affect the application of&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">Chapters V and VA of the Penal Code; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the Evidence Act or any other law or practice regarding the admissibility of evidence.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12J-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;To avoid doubt, subsection (2) does not affect the liability of an unincorporated association or a partnership for an offence under this Act, and applies whether or not the unincorporated association or partnership is convicted of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12J-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section —<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“officer”, in relation to an unincorporated association (other than a partnership), means the president, the secretary, or any member of the committee of the unincorporated association, and includes —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any person holding a position analogous to that of president, secretary or member of a committee of the unincorporated association; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any person purporting to act in any such capacity;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“partner” includes a person purporting to act as a partner;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“state of mind” of a person includes —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the knowledge, intention, opinion, belief or purpose of the person; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the person’s reasons for the intention, opinion, belief or purpose.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12K-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Composition of offences</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12K.</strong><a name="pr12K-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Director-General or an authorised officer may compound any offence under this Act that is prescribed as a compoundable offence by collecting from a person reasonably suspected of having committed the offence a sum not exceeding the lower of the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">one half of the amount of the maximum fine that is prescribed for the offence;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">$2,000.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr12K-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;On payment of the sum of money, no further proceedings are to be taken against that person in respect of the offence.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr12K-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;All sums collected under this section must be paid into the Consolidated Fund.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12L-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Jurisdiction of courts</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12L.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;Despite the Criminal Procedure Code, a District Court or a Magistrate’s Court has jurisdiction to try any offence under this Act and has power to impose the full punishment for that offence.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr13-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Reward to informer</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>13.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The court may direct any fine or any portion of any fine imposed or levied under this Act to be paid to the informer.<div class="pREProvNo">[12</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr14-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Fees, etc., payable to Board</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>14.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;All fees, charges and moneys collected under this Act  (except composition sums) must be paid to the Board.<div class="amendNote">[Act 10 of 2019 wef 01/04/2019]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr15-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Form and giving of notices and other documents</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>15.</strong><a name="pr15-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;All notices and other documents of any nature that the Director-General is empowered to give under this Act may —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">be in any form the Director-General thinks fit; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">subject to the direction of the Director-General, be given by an authorised officer on behalf of the Director-General.</td></tr></tbody></table></span><a name="pr15-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Where any notice or document mentioned in subsection (1) requires authentication, the signature (or an official facsimile of the signature) of the Director-General or an authorised officer affixed to the notice or document is sufficient authentication.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr16-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Inaccuracies in notices and other documents</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>16.</strong><a name="pr16-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;A misnomer or an inaccurate description of any wildlife, person, place, article or conveyance named or described in any notice or other document prepared, issued or served under, by reason of or for the purposes of this Act does not in any way affect the operation of this Act as respects that wildlife, person, place, article or conveyance if that wildlife, person, place, article or conveyance is so designated in the notice or other document as to be identifiable.</span><a name="pr16-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;Proceedings taken under or by reason of this Act are not invalid for want of form.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr17-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Evidence</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>17.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;A document purporting to be under the hand of the Director-General or an enforcement officer on any matter or thing in connection with the administration or enforcement of, or any investigation carried out under, this Act is admissible as evidence in any proceedings under this Act and is prima facie evidence of the facts stated in the document.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr18-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Protection from personal liability</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>18.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;No liability shall lie against the Director-General or an enforcement officer, or any person acting under the direction of the Director-General or an enforcement officer, for anything which is done or purported to be done, or omitted to be done, in good faith and with reasonable care in —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the exercise or purported exercise of any power under this Act; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the performance or purported performance of any function under this Act.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr19-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Service of documents</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>19.</strong><a name="pr19-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;A document that is permitted or required by this Act to be served on a person may be served as described in this section.</span><a name="pr19-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;A document permitted or required by this Act to be served on an individual may be served —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by giving it to the individual personally;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by sending it by prepaid registered post to the address specified by the individual for the service of documents or, if no address is so specified, the individual’s residential address or business address;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by leaving it at the individual’s residential address with an adult apparently resident there, or at the individual’s business address with an adult apparently employed there;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by affixing a copy of the document in a conspicuous place at the individual’s residential address or business address;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by sending it by fax to the fax number last known to the person giving or serving the document as the fax number for the service of documents on the individual; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>f</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by sending it by email to the individual’s last email address.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr19-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;A document permitted or required by this Act to be served on a partnership (other than a limited liability partnership) may be served&nbsp;—<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by giving it to any partner or other similar officer of the partnership;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by leaving it at, or by sending it by prepaid registered post to, the partnership’s business address;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by sending it by fax to the fax number used at the partnership’s business address; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by sending it by email to the partnership’s last email address.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr19-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&nbsp;&nbsp;A document permitted or required by this Act to be served on a body corporate (including a limited liability partnership) or an unincorporated association may be served —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by giving it to the secretary or other similar officer of the body corporate or unincorporated association, or the limited liability partnership’s manager;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by leaving it at, or by sending it by prepaid registered post to, the body corporate’s or unincorporated association’s registered office or principal office in Singapore;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by sending it by fax to the fax number used at the body corporate’s or unincorporated association’s registered office or principal office in Singapore; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by sending it by email to the body corporate’s or unincorporated association’s last email address.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr19-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&nbsp;&nbsp;Service of a document under this section takes effect —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">if the document is sent by fax and a notification of successful transmission is received, on the day of transmission;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">if the document is sent by email, at the time that the email becomes capable of being retrieved by the person to whom it is sent; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">if the document is sent by prepaid registered post, 2 days after the day the document was posted (even if it is returned undelivered).</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr19-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&nbsp;&nbsp;However, service of any document under this Act on a person by email may be effected only with the person’s prior consent to service in that way.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr19-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&nbsp;&nbsp;This section does not apply to documents to be served in proceedings in court.</td></tr></tbody></table><a name="pr19-ps8-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(8)&nbsp;&nbsp;In this section —<table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“business address” means —<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in the case of an individual, the individual’s usual or last known place of business in Singapore; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in the case of a partnership (other than a limited liability partnership), the partnership’s principal or last known place of business in Singapore;</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“last email address” means the last email address given by the addressee concerned to the person giving or serving the document as the email address for the service of documents under this Act;</td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="def" style="font-size:13pt">“residential address” means an individual’s usual or last known place of residence in Singapore.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr20-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Exemption</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>20.</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may, by order in the <em>Gazette</em>, exempt any person, place or wildlife, or any class of persons, places or wildlife, from all or any of the provisions of this Act, either generally or in a particular case and subject to any condition the Minister may impose.<div class="amendNote">[Act 18 of 2020 wef 01/06/2020]</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr21-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Rules</span></td></tr></tbody></table><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>21.</strong><a name="pr21-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">—(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;The Minister may make rules necessary or convenient to be prescribed for carrying out or giving effect to this Act.</span><a name="pr21-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;In particular, the Minister may make rules for all or any of the following:<table class="p1_1" style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tbody><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the
